Current Commentary

Five Nations Sending Financial Experts to China 28

— Ji

According to a recent London dispatch, the governments of the United Kingdom, the United States, France, Italy, and Japan have reached an agreement to each send financial representatives to China to investigate the state of our country's currency. The candidates from the UK and France have already been officially announced. Representatives from the United States, Italy, and Japan will also be appointed soon. Although this matter is still developing, and we cannot predict its future success, the Chinese economy has recently been greatly affected by the US silver policy, exhibiting extreme instability. The governments of various countries are concerned about this and are sending representatives to China to investigate our real situation and offer their contributions. Regardless of their future methods or purposes, this kind of international sympathy towards us is indeed worthy of our approval.

As a result of the high degree of development of capitalism, the world economy has long been integrated and inseparable. The safety or danger of one corner is always enough to affect the overall situation. Therefore, for the sake of progress in international peace and interests, cooperation and mutual assistance in all aspects are also very urgent. It is a fact that our country has been in a state of disrepair in recent years due to economic panic. We are unwilling to avoid treatment. Therefore, the Chinese people have expressed considerable welcome to the economic investigation teams from various countries coming to China. This is because China is currently in a period of awaiting many things to be handled, and all kinds of construction matters rely on the material and technical assistance of various countries. However, "using foreign power" is by no means the same as "relying on foreign power." Currency is the center of a country's economic life, and its impact on national independence and survival is very great. It must not be subject to the constraints of other countries. At present, the great powers often use their financial policies to rule over various weak and small national countries, such as the United States in Cuba and the United Kingdom in Sweden, Norway, Denmark, and other countries. If, as reported by foreign telegrams, representatives of various countries all want to bring Chinese currency under their own sphere of influence, is this not intended to compete for economic leadership in the Far East?

We believe that the reform of China's monetary system is an extremely difficult matter. We should exhaust the wisdom of the entire nation, carefully consider the interests of all parties, make meticulous plans, and prepare thorough arrangements. It cannot be achieved by "building a house based on roadside advice." Moreover, since China is an independent country, no matter how the currency is reformed, it should have an independent currency position. It should not have any currency connection with any country, nor should it be tempted or threatened by any country to compromise. Otherwise, China may become a colony of the great powers in terms of finance, and the self-reliance and prosperity of the national economy will be even more difficult. Recently, Sir Frederick Whyte in England published an article in London saying that "China's survival depends solely on the strength of its national power." These words are truly worthy of our deep reflection.

Britain and Japan Exchange Views on Investigating Chinese Finance 29

(London) Regarding the issue of Japan refusing to participate in the discussion of currency problems in the Chinese capital, it is known from Far East sources that Japan is not opposed to the principle of discussing currency problems, but believes that this kind of discussion is not very appropriate under the current circumstances. Only after financial experts from Britain and France have completed a preliminary investigation of China's currency situation, and after Sino-Japanese relations are smoother, will they send financial experts to China. In fact, this matter is being exchanged between the Japanese Embassy and the British Foreign Office, and the Japanese government has not yet made a final decision. (19th Havas Dispatch)

Japan's Next Year's Budget: Military First Doctrine, Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Policy Towards China and Russia Completely Consistent with the Military 30

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Finance is currently preparing the budget for the 11th year of Showa. Finance Minister Takahashi will explain its contents at the cabinet meeting on the 21st. It is reported that the budget preparation policy for next year adopts the doctrine of putting national defense first. (19th Japan United News Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Okada met with reporters at noon today and made the following statement: The harmony between finance and national defense is the most important thing. Whether the budget is increased or decreased is not a problem. The key is how to harmonize finance and national defense. Japan is currently active, and necessary expenses cannot be reduced, so there is no one who advocates reducing national defense expenditures. Judging from the current state of Japanese finance, national defense expenditures are not without being too heavy. However, it is indeed a necessary thing for national security and national defense. However, the issuing power of public bonds is limited, and the national economy cannot be endangered for this purpose. Therefore, it is necessary to harmonize finance and national defense. This issue will be carefully reviewed by the cabinet review committee and the investigation committee. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the military have completely consistent opinions on the policy towards China, and the same is true for the policy towards Russia. (19th Japan United News Dispatch)

Japanese Foreign Minister Seeks to Adjust Relations with Russia, Plans to Demand Withdrawal of Red Army Stationed in the Far East as a Precondition for Signing a Non-Aggression Treaty, Russian Ambassador Visits Takahashi to Inquire About True Intentions 31

(Tokyo) Because relations between Japan and Russia have improved since the establishment of the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Foreign Minister Hirota plans to permanently preserve this state. He is preparing to propose to Russia a plan for the establishment of a border dispute mediation committee, demanding the removal of the Red Army's defense work on the border, and the withdrawal of troops stationed in the Far East, as a preliminary condition for the signing of a non-aggression treaty. Ambassador Ota, stationed in Russia, attended the Paris ambassador meeting and has now returned to his post in Moscow. The Foreign Minister will instruct him to begin negotiations with the Russian government in the near future. According to the Foreign Minister's opinion, the atmosphere between Japan and Russia has improved. It is meaningless for the Soviet Union to send 300,000 troops to the Far Eastern border area, and it is harmful. The Japanese-Russian military conflict in the Suifenhe area the other day may occur again in the future. Now the Soviet Union should take the only measure, which is to withdraw or reduce its unnecessary troops stationed in the Far East. The Foreign Minister plans to advise our government to implement troop withdrawal, and then negotiate the peaceful handling of the border. This negotiation will be conducted by Ambassador Ota with Litvinov. (19th Japan United News Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Soviet Russian Ambassador Yurenev to Japan visited Finance Minister Takahashi at 1:30 this afternoon. The content of the meeting seemed to be because the Finance Minister made a statement at the cabinet review meeting on the 17th, hoping to conclude a Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty, so he inquired about the Finance Minister's true intentions. (19th Den Tsushin Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The Soviet Russian ambassador to Japan visited Finance Minister Takahashi this afternoon to exchange views on Japanese-Russian relations. The meeting lasted for 40 minutes. Mr. Yurenev stated his opinions as follows: For the sake of maintaining peace in the Far East, and also world peace, it is the only way to increase the welfare of both countries for Japan and Russia to cooperate and strive for harmony and friendship in both political and economic aspects in the future. Fortunately, the problem of the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway has been resolved, and there is currently no conflict of interests between the two countries. Therefore, with Your Excellency's efforts in the future, friendly relations can be promoted, and it is hoped that the time for Japan and Russia to conclude a non-aggression treaty will arrive quickly. He questioned the Finance Minister's opinion. Finance Minister Takahashi replied: I deeply agree with your Excellency's opinion. In short, the major issue of concluding a non-aggression treaty cannot be resolved overnight. It is only possible to reach that time after the various pending issues between the two countries have been resolved satisfactorily. He hopes that the two countries will cooperate with each other to promote friendly relations on political and economic issues, and after various earnest talks, the meeting ended at 2:15 pm. (19th Den Tsushin Dispatch)

Tokyo According to a report from Ambassador Ota stationed in Russia, Ambassador Ota visited the Deputy Minister of People's Affairs of the Soviet Union on the 17th, requesting a formal reply to the memorandum on revising the fisheries treaty submitted by the Japanese government, and urged the Russian government to start negotiations as soon as possible. However, the Russian Deputy Minister used the excuse of careful study of the Japanese memorandum, attempting to delay it. (19th Japan United News Dispatch)

Hardships of Farmers in Liaoning, Famine Throughout Qingyuan and Xingjing, Joining the Volunteer Army, Japanese Army Worried 32

(Shenyang) According to a survey, of the 28 counties in Liaoning Province (which have been changed administrative regions), 8 counties have surplus grain, 9 counties are self-sufficient, and the remaining 9 counties lack food. Qingyuan County is the worst, with a population of 68,000, with no food available, desperately picking leaves and grass roots to fill their hunger, a miserable sight. Xingjing County, with a population of 70,000, is also the same, with famine victims everywhere. Although the "Manchu" authorities slightly provide a small amount of sorghum, it is not enough to eat. Farmers have joined the volunteer army one after another, and the Japanese army is quite worried. (19th China Allied News Dispatch)

Situation in East Africa Rapidly Deteriorating, Unprecedented Military Parade in the Capital of Abyssinia, King Abyssinia Personally Inspects Strong Military Appearance, Regular Army Five Times Stronger Than Before, Italy Decides to Mobilize Two Divisions to East Africa 33

Stabilizing International Currencies, Britain is Actually an Obstacle, US Treasury Helps France Maintain the Status of the Franc, Willing to See the World Return to the Gold Standard 34

(Washington) According to reliable sources here today, the United States is very willing to fix the US currency at the current exchange rate. This assistance to France to maintain the franc indicates that the United States is willing to see the world return to the gold standard. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau stated yesterday that this move by the United States is reasonable. It is said that the obstacle to currency stability now is actually Britain, because Britain is unwilling to have any changes in its currency system before the election. (18th Guomin News Dispatch)

(Washington) The general public believes that the US Treasury Department's sale of US dollars to help the franc the other day shows that the United States is willing to determine the existing value of the dollar internationally. A certain government official (who does not want his name to be officially announced) said, "If France is forced to abandon the gold standard, it must first reduce the value of the currency, and its impact will inevitably lead to a competition for currency devaluation among countries, and the priority position occupied by the United States in international trade will also be lost. Senator Pittman, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, explained the Treasury Department's assistance to the franc, saying, "The path to international exchange market stability has been further advanced by this." (18th Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) Mr. Daenery, the president of the Bank of France, issued a telegram at the meeting of the presidents of central banks of various countries in Basel, Switzerland the other day, saying that after the government obtains full power, it will be used to make up for the budget deficit and restore national credit. From then on, the currencies of various countries can be expected to be generally stabilized, and business relations can also be expected to return to normal. Financial figures here attach great importance to the significance of this declaration. Mr. Daenery also said that during the recent period of financial panic in France, both the United Kingdom and the United States provided assistance. As for the Bank of France repeatedly raising the discount rate, its purpose is nothing more than to prevent speculative behavior. (18th Havas Dispatch)

Anglo-German Naval Agreement Quickly Signed and Announced, Eden to Go to France on Friday to Explain, Italian and Russian Experts Also to Be Invited to England 35

(London) The terms of the Anglo-German Naval Agreement are detailed in the White Paper published today. The documents exchanged between the two governments feel that a good thing has been accomplished, but their work has not aroused much excitement in France. The Parisian newspapers have expressed dissatisfaction loudly. It is heard that the French government's note to the British government regarding the agreement will indicate that France intends to have a higher shipbuilding program. At the same time, British Minister of Disarmament Eden will go to Paris on Friday to discuss naval issues and the general situation in Europe with the French government. One of the most important points of the Anglo-German Naval Agreement is that Britain allows Germany to have the right to place submarines in a tonnage equivalent to that of Britain. However, Germany promises not to exceed 45% of this type of warship except in extraordinary circumstances. If it needs to exceed, it must first consult with the British government. The British government said that this agreement will be of great importance to future naval restrictions, and it is believed that it can make it easier to establish a general compromise among the naval countries of the world. The ratio of Germany occupying 35% of the total tonnage of the British Navy is a permanent ratio and will not change due to the construction of warships by other countries. However, when there is a major reversal in the current balance of international forces, Germany can invite Britain to reconsider the new situation. If there are any changes in the future international naval situation, the allocation of tonnage for various types of warships that have been negotiated can be modified by the two governments through consultation. General Ribbentrop, the German representative, expressed his delight when the British government accepted this condition, saying that this agreement is permanent, practical, and will take effect immediately. However, France does not think so. The Tribune said that the agreement has put the German navy on an equal footing with France, and the parliament has to increase the construction of warships. The semi-official Times said that Germany allowed London to negotiate separately on two issues of great importance to British security, namely sky armaments and sea armaments, in order to split the Stresa Front of Britain, France, and Italy. General public opinion in France believes that Britain's permission for Germany to re-establish a navy equivalent to 35% of the British navy is a big mistake and will inevitably seriously affect its own security and world peace. Reuters diplomatic correspondent claimed that the clause in the Anglo-German Naval Agreement that is most noteworthy to London is the one regarding submarines. It is believed that British naval experts now hope that the concession given to Germany by Britain here can prevent Germany from building aircraft carriers. (18th Reuters Dispatch)

(London) The sudden establishment of a naval agreement between Britain and Germany has caused people to worry about the cooperative relationship between Britain, France, and Italy. France and Italy are not in favor of this move by Britain. However, Britain said that its actions were not intended to condone Germany's actions to violate the Treaty of Versailles. According to reliable sources, there is a secret condition attached to this treaty, that is, Germany guarantees not to build aircraft carriers. The Anglo-German Naval Agreement was signed by Foreign Secretary Hoare on the British side and by Hitler's representative Ribbentrop on the German side. After signing this treaty, Hoare claimed that the signing of this treaty is sufficient to promote the resolution of general naval issues. (18th Guomin News Dispatch)

(London) After the establishment of the Anglo-German Naval Agreement, representatives from Britain and Germany will hold talks to discuss Germany's shipbuilding program. These talks will continue until the end of the week. Germany's shipbuilding program will be completed within seven years according to the 35% ratio. (19th Hanes Dispatch)

(London) Although the Anglo-German naval talks have reached a compromise, they still need to continue to resolve the details regarding shipbuilding. France has now been invited to send experts to London to participate in the discussion to prepare for the holding of a major naval conference. Italy and Russia also appear to be invited to send experts here. (19th Reuters Dispatch)

Content of Anglo-German Agreement, Representatives of Both Sides Exchange Notes to Confirm 36

(Berlin) Efforts to limit armaments and ease the political situation have made preliminary practical achievements in London today, because the Anglo-German Naval Conference has reached complete agreement and signed a naval convention. The full text of the agreement has been published simultaneously in London and Berlin tonight. This agreement has been confirmed by the exchange of documents by British Foreign Secretary Hoare and Special Envoy Ribbentrop. The content of the documents is as follows:

(1) The German government's proposal that Germany's navy should account for 35% of the British sea tonnage in the future has been accepted by the British government. The British government recognizes that this proposal will make an important contribution to future naval restrictions, and believes that the Anglo-German agreement, which takes effect from today, is the final agreement signed by the two countries and is conducive to the signing of general naval treaties by various naval countries.

(2) The British government subsequently endorsed the German representative's declaration on the implementation of this principle. The summary of this declaration is as follows: (A) The number of 35% is a naval ratio of a permanent nature. The total tonnage of the German navy will never exceed 35% of the British Empire fleet, as stipulated in the treaty. If there are no explicit restrictions on this tonnage in the future, it will never exceed 35% of the actual total tonnage.

(B) If a general naval agreement is established in the future, and the relative naval strength of each country is not specified, then Germany will not insist on including this ratio in the agreement, provided that other countries fully guarantee the maintenance of this ratio.

(C) Under any circumstances, Germany will maintain a ratio of 35%, but if other countries expand their navies indefinitely and disrupt the past naval balance, the German government reserves the right to invite the British government to consider the new situation.

(D) The German government advocates dividing battleships into several categories, and stipulating the maximum tonnage and maximum caliber of artillery for each type, and the German government accepts the ratio of 25% for various types of battleships, and is willing to modify this ratio according to the general naval treaty in the future. If a general naval agreement cannot be established in the future, the German government's right to change the 35% ratio shall be adjusted by a bilateral agreement between the German and British governments.

(E) If other countries want to combine cruisers and destroyers into one category, Germany can also do the same. However, Germany advocates classifying such ships.

(F) As for submarines, the total tonnage of all German submarines should be equal to the total tonnage of British submarines, but it will never exceed 35% of the total tonnage of the British Navy. Germany is willing to limit its total submarine tonnage to 45% of that of Britain, but it reserves the right to exceed 45% in case of emergency, but is also willing to negotiate this matter with the British government in advance.

(G) If it is impossible to apply the ratio of 35% to various types of warships, the tonnage of one type of warship should be transferred to other types of warships, so that Germany can make full use of its tonnage. However, this should be subject to the special agreement of the two governments, but it should not exceed the ratio of 35 to 100.

(3) The British government has learned of the reservations in the declaration and recognizes its right to agree to maintain the number of 35%. The two governments have no objection to this. In the letter, Ribbentrop also stated that the German government also recognizes that the Anglo-German Naval Agreement is the final valid agreement signed by the two governments, and it will take effect from today and will be able to promote the conclusion of general naval agreements by various countries. (18th Guomin News Dispatch)

Eden to Visit France on Friday; Laval Expresses Welcome 37

(Paris) British Ambassador to France, Sir Clerk, this morning presented Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval with the full text of the Anglo-German naval agreement and reported to Laval that British representative to the League of Nations, Eden, will come to France on Friday to discuss general European and specific issues with the French government. Laval immediately expressed his welcome to Eden's visit to France. After the British Ambassador left the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Laval had a lengthy conversation with the Soviet Ambassador. According to well-informed sources, the two also discussed the Anglo-French naval agreement. This morning, newspapers competed to publish the Anglo-German naval agreement, along with detailed critiques. Nationalist newspapers heavily criticized Britain for negotiating with Germany alone, which dealt a blow to general conferences and the collective security system, claiming that the "Stresa Front" has finally been broken. They further stated that the large number of German submarines stipulated in the agreement is particularly disadvantageous to France, forcing France to increase its navy in the event of disputes with other countries. The newspapers also expressed regret that Italy has obtained a new opportunity to contend for naval supremacy with France, and warned that the restoration of the German fleet will cause unrest in the Baltic Sea, questioning why Britain does not alleviate this unrest for the continent. Bodinat, the international telegraph editor of the Paris Echo, also sternly criticized the British government and demanded that future naval negotiations be held in Paris, as Britain has disregarded French interests and France can no longer recognize Britain as an arbitrator. (National News Agency dispatch, 19th)

(Paris) The French government responded yesterday to the British note regarding the Anglo-German naval talks in London. The main points of the response are reportedly as follows:

(1) The French reply stated that it is inappropriate to separate the naval issue from the overall arms issue.

(2) The reply stated that the objective of the Anglo-French joint declaration in London on February 2 was to comprehensively resolve all arms issues within the framework of a security system.

(3) France will have to determine the standard for its future naval construction plans based on the rate at which Germany implements its shipbuilding plan.

(4) The reply also requested clarification on how Germany will deal with the situation if the Soviet Union builds a navy. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

(London) Minister without Portfolio Eden is about to go to Paris to conduct talks with the French government. The Daily Telegraph reported that the objectives of the talks are roughly the following four items: (1) Germany has submitted a note to the signatories of the Locarno Treaty, stating that the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance pact conflicts with the obligations stipulated in the Locarno Treaty, which should be jointly answered by the signatories; (2) Whether there is any possibility of promoting negotiations on an "air Locarno" at present; (3) What new steps should be taken to seek a peaceful resolution to the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia; (4) Whether there is progress on the issue of holding a security conference for the countries in the Danube River basin. In addition, Eden will invite French naval experts to Britain to prepare for Anglo-French naval talks, which will be attended by experts from Italy and the Soviet Union. Furthermore, Prime Minister Baldwin plans to attend the general assembly and executive council meetings of the League of Nations in September of this year. (Havas dispatch, 19th)

(London) Minister without Portfolio Eden is scheduled to go to Paris on Friday to discuss naval issues with the French government. It is evident that Britain is eager to explain the actual results of the Anglo-German naval agreement to France. British people are very satisfied that the agreement will prevent Britain and Germany from engaging in naval competition in the North Sea as they did before 1914. Regarding submarines, it is generally believed that although Britain did not allow Germany to have submarine tonnage equal to Britain's, Germany has agreed that in peacetime, its submarine tonnage will not exceed 45% of Britain's. If the submarine tonnage exceeds 35%, the tonnage of other classes of warships must be reduced, which may also prevent Germany from building aircraft carriers. From an international perspective, the Anglo-German naval agreement has brought Germany back into the collective security system. Therefore, the naval agreement does not conflict with the policies advocated in the Anglo-French declaration of February 3 and the Stresa Conference communiqué. In addition, although Italy and France have objections to the Anglo-German naval agreement, submitting the German proposal to all countries for general discussion would likely delay the conclusion of the agreement and cause Germany to change its original proposal. As for whether France and Italy will change their naval construction plans in the future, Germany may not be able to immediately increase its naval tonnage, as Germany must obtain Britain's consent beforehand if it needs to increase its naval tonnage, which is clearly stated in the white paper. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

Observations from French Political Circles: Likely to Promote Air Force Convention 38

(Paris) French political figures believe that the Anglo-German naval agreement is likely to impact the hope for the establishment of an air force convention. They feel it is inappropriate to independently conclude a naval agreement without progress on the issue of a general security system. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

(London) After the conclusion of the Anglo-German naval agreement, it is rumored that the chief German representative, Ribbentrop, had talks with Minister without Portfolio Eden and proposed the conclusion of an air agreement with content similar to the naval agreement. However, what people can generally confirm is that the talks between Ribbentrop and Eden concerned matters other than naval issues, and not necessarily the air convention issue. Eden is scheduled to go to Paris on Friday, at which time he will inform French Prime Minister Laval of the results of the exchange of views between Britain and Germany. (Havas dispatch, 19th)

(Paris) The nationalist newspaper "Le Peuple" today commented on the Anglo-German naval agreement, with the title "The Death of the Stresa Spirit," saying that Britain's current action of snubbing France and Italy and making Germany complacent is difficult to understand. Smaller newspapers said that this agreement is a major victory for Germany, sufficient to strengthen Hitler's position in Europe, and is the most serious incident, enough to cause major disputes in Anglo-French relations. "Le Petit Parisien" said that the meaning of this agreement is that Germany's naval power will always be weaker than Britain's, so Britain spared no effort to achieve this unexpected great deal with the fastest means. Therefore, after the conclusion of this agreement, the position of the British cabinet will become more solid. Eden's mission to France seems to be to explain the alarm caused by the sudden conclusion of the Anglo-German naval agreement to the French. "Le Petit Journal" said that although this is a major victory for Hitler, it is also an achievement of the British Navy seizing the opportunity to benefit itself. (National News Agency dispatch, 19th)

British Public Opinion Expresses Satisfaction; Prelude to German Arms Equality 39

(London) Members of Parliament have expressed satisfaction with the Anglo-German naval agreement. The opposition believes that this is a prelude to granting Germany complete equal rights in armaments. Most parliamentarians also see it as fortunate, believing that Britain's naval superiority in the North Sea can be maintained for some time as a result. The British cabinet has also gained a good pretext in election tactics, considering it a tool for victory. Therefore, the early rescheduling of the House of Commons election is an expected event. (Havas dispatch, 19th)

(London) The Anglo-German naval agreement has been welcomed in principle by newspapers today. The Times stated that both sides are willing to reach an understanding, so both sides have made concessions. The result is at least better than before 1914. The Morning Post stated that this agreement is indeed a satisfactory document in some respects, but it does not contain provisions limiting the number and tonnage of German submarines. Britain did not consult the signatories of the naval treaty before taking this step. The Daily Telegraph stated that it would have been more prudent for the British government to inform the French government of its views first, but this agreement can serve as the basis for more general negotiations in the future. The News Chronicle stated that this agreement is a major event in history and the first document in which postwar Germany has participated in arms limitation. The Daily Express stated that this agreement greatly contributes to disarmament and public peace. The Daily Mail stated that this agreement is a commitment by Britain and Germany not to engage in naval competition, so it is welcome. (Reuters dispatch, 19th)

(London) The Daily Telegraph commented on the importance of the Anglo-German naval agreement, saying, "Germany's rearmament and the expansion of navies by countries in Europe and the Far East have created a new situation, and the North Sea has once again become an important strategic location. All of this has forced Britain to change its naval policy. Britain currently has 45 submarines, totaling 55,244 tons. By the end of next year, some of these will no longer be applicable, and this tonnage will be reduced to 52,700 tons. If calculated at 35%, Germany can build submarines up to 19,635 tons. However, the 12 submarines currently under construction, each of 250 tons, are not included in this figure. Furthermore, according to news from Germany, the country does not intend to build submarines of more than 800 tons in the coming years." (Havas dispatch, 19th)

Hitler's Peace Policy: German Newspapers Consider it a Great Success 40

(Berlin) The Nazi Party's official newspaper commented on the Anglo-German naval agreement today, considering it a major event related to the European situation. All previous disarmament negotiations in Europe have failed, but the success of this Anglo-German naval agreement has established a good model for the issue of disarmament. Moreover, this is a practical step for leader Hitler to open up the chaotic situation in Europe and establish a peaceful policy. Therefore, the conclusion of this agreement proves that with the sincerity of mutual understanding, any political problem can be easily resolved. Hitler's peace policy has swept away all rumors and suspicions about Anglo-German naval competition, and using only 35% of the British navy as Germany's coastal defense is the basis for Anglo-German understanding. The newspaper continued, "Hitler is a frank politician in Europe and has already achieved results because of this. As before, there was the success of rapprochement with Poland, and now there is the beginning of Anglo-German coordination, which are all the results of his peaceful advocacy and his ability to implement his advocacy." (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Responsible Sources in Vienna: Believe British Policy Unchanged 41

Vienna Responsible sources believe that after the conclusion of the Anglo-German naval agreement, Britain's general policy will not change. Although the German side is making great efforts to promote that Britain and Germany have reached a final agreement in London, sources here believe that the Anglo-German naval agreement should still be subordinate to the general naval agreement. In addition, Britain will continue to pursue its policy of consolidating international security organizations. A commentary in the "Daily Newspaper" stated, "The united front of Britain, France, and Italy established by the Stresa Conference is in no danger of breaking apart. Germany's victory is only superficial." (Havas dispatch, 19th)

Yugoslav Prime Minister Prepares to Meet Mussolini; Small Entente Representative Visits Italy 42

(Rome) Yugoslav Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Jevtić will soon meet with representatives of the Italian government, or perhaps even with Prime Minister Mussolini. Mussolini has now left Rome for Romagna for vacation, and it is possible that he will meet Jevtić there. It should be noted that Jevtić was originally scheduled to meet with Undersecretary Suvich in Venice on the 19th of last month, but Jevtić was unable to leave due to domestic political reasons in Yugoslavia, and the discussion was cancelled. What we should pay attention to is that Jevtić will be the chairman of the Small Entente Political Council at the end of this month, so he will visit Italy as a representative of the three countries of the Small Entente, and not just representing Yugoslavia. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

French Cabinet Decides to Dismiss Soldiers; Sign of Easing Tensions with Germany 43

(Paris) The French cabinet decided today that, starting from July 16, all conscripts who complete their service in mid-April will be completely dismissed. The cabinet said that this move is intended to save money, but observers also believe that this is a sign that the situation with Germany has eased. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Inmates Mutiny in Lansing, Michigan Prison; Demand Improved Food and Removal of Prison Doctor; Attempt to Seize Weapons Repelled by Tear Gas 44

Lansing, Michigan Today, 380 inmates in a state-run coal mine here mutinied 720 feet underground, cutting all telephone lines to the surface, leaving only one line connected to the armory. There are four guards in the armory. It is reported that the prisoners attempted to break in but were repelled by tear gas. They are now planning to try again to seize weapons. All mine entrances have been blocked. There are still eleven guards in the mine who have been detained by the prisoners. They also set fire near the armory in an attempt to smoke out the guards inside. According to the prisoners' representatives, who spoke to prison officials on the phone, the reason for the mutiny is to demand improved food and the removal of prison doctor Packer, because two inmates who suffered from appendicitis last month died after Packer performed surgery. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Trotsky Moves from France to Norway; Prohibited from Any Political Activity 45

Oslo, Norway Former Soviet Red Army leader Trotsky, who has been living in exile, has arrived here today. Trotsky had been residing in France but was accused by French right-wing newspapers last year of instigating the February 6 riots. The French government then ordered him to leave the country, but later allowed him to stay in France, but only allowed his movements to a certain location and prohibited him from participating in any political activities. This time, he has obtained permission from the Norwegian authorities to reside for three months, but he must also refrain from any political activity. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Italian Government Revokes Order to Recall Silver Coins; Only Applies to 10-Lira and 20-Lira Coins 46

(Rome) The government recently ordered the recall of silver coins circulating in the market to be exchanged for banknotes, using these silver coins as reserves. It is now known that this measure only applies to 10-lira and 20-lira silver coins. As for 5-lira coins, they will not be recalled. The total amount of silver coins in circulation is 1,635,000,000 lire, of which 5-lira coins account for 808,000,000 lire. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

International Commercial Telegraph – Special Business Report from Reuters, June 19 47

Gold and Silver The London gold price today was 140 shillings and 11.5 pence, down half a penny.

London bullion The silver market was soft today. The spot price was 32 pence and 1875, and the futures price was 32 pence and 4375, both down half a penny. India and China sold, while the United States and speculators bought when prices fell. The market closed quietly.

Wounded Tree Big Article Silver market futures prices fell because silver prices in Bombay and London both fell. At the opening, September fell 75 pounds.

Exchange Rates In the London foreign exchange market, there was little trading this morning. The US dollar was firmer, and the French franc was mostly inactive. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was $4.93625, which was six hundredths and five thousandths lower than yesterday's closing price. One hour later, it continued to fall one thousand eight hundred and seventy five ten thousandths of a cent. In the afternoon, there was a turnaround and it rose six hundred twenty five ten thousandths of a cent to $4.935. This price did not change until 2 o'clock, which was higher than the opening price.

British-French The opening rose nine pounds to 74 francs 68. It continued to drop three pounds within the first hour. There was no movement at noon, but there were slight fluctuations later. The afternoon 2 o'clock price was 74 francs 68, the same as the opening price.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton This morning was quiet. The July futures opening price was 11.5, which was one point higher than yesterday's closing price. The trend was mixed, and prices showed signs of weakness. It is heard that the weather in the cotton belt is gradually improving.

Rubber

Securities

New York Securities opened with stable prices. Some stocks rose slightly due to slight changes in the bill to abolish public utility bank companies. Traders believe that the American Copper Industry Association's resolution to cooperate to maintain existing standards is a favorable factor for securities. Air Force Competition Between France and Germany 73

— Berlin Correspondence

"The future of Germany lies in maritime development," was the warning of former German Emperor Wilhelm II when he wanted to expand the navy, and it was also one aspect of the German national spirit before the European War. Now, Air Force Chief General Göring is loudly proclaiming, "Germany's destiny lies in the air!" To resolutely express his nation's determination, he has implemented "Aeronautical Mechanics" as a major course in all schools above the middle school level nationwide. However, simply talking about "Aeronautical Mechanics" is just empty talk, not the habit of the German people, and also not suitable for practical application. Therefore, they have gamified aviation. There are thirty national aviation game fields, and several thousand gliders (invented by the German Lilienthal) without engines. Eight thousand young people are practicing flying skills and learning glider operation. The Department of Aviation divides them into three levels: A, B, and C. Among them, the highest level, C, has no fewer than a thousand people whose skills can compete with those in France. In the future, many excellent aviators will inevitably emerge from these young people, and they will all be soldiers of the German Air Force.

Germany now has 260 airfields, of which 124 are ordinary commercial airfields, and the rest are military. The exact number of aircraft in Germany and its aircraft manufacturing capacity have not yet been publicly announced. According to the estimate of French Army Chief of Staff General Maurin, German aircraft factories can build fifteen fighter jets every day. According to the estimation of Soviet Deputy People's Commissar for Defense Tukhachevsky, Germany currently has 3,700 military aircraft, 8,000 flying officers, and 52,000 airmen. In addition, 60,000 people have been selected and are undergoing rigorous airmen training. According to British estimates, Germany has about 1,700 aircraft, of which 600 are training aircraft, and the rest are scattered in various airfields, extremely secret and difficult for outsiders to see. Another noteworthy thing is that the number of workers at the Krupp factory has increased to 25,000. Whether they are manufacturing weapons, military supplies, or other things is also a mystery. Since the establishment of the Department of Aviation in 1928, France has strived for the unification of the air force. Except for the aircraft carried by naval aircraft carriers and the non-carrier-based aircraft belonging to the Naval Association, all are under the command of the Department of Aviation to form a huge air force. The strength of the French land-based air force includes 48 reconnaissance squadrons, 33 fighter squadrons, 32 bomber squadrons, and 18 balloon squadrons, with approximately 31,000 soldiers. The current total number of land-based aircraft is approximately 3,000, which will expand to 5,400 in wartime. At present, the promotion of civil aviation is being vigorously promoted, and the units under the Department of Aviation will also expand from the current 131 squadrons to 156 squadrons.

In terms of the current situation, the French Air Force certainly has an absolute advantage over Germany. However, natural resources are not very abundant, and the "human element" is even more inferior compared to Germany. It is necessary to find ways to supplement and reverse the current decline. Therefore, French politicians and diplomats, feeling disappointed after Germany gradually developed upward and withdrew from the League of Nations, and having some contradictions with Italy, had no choice but to turn to pull the Soviet Union into the League of Nations, and at the same time want it to become France's ally. Because the current Soviet fighter jets have increased three and a half times compared to four years ago, the flight speed has also doubled, and the effective combat radius has increased three times. The number of aircraft is not very detailed, but it is more than 2,000, and the remaining mechanized troops are no less than those of other European countries. However, the French General Staff still generally adheres to the saying "Adequate preparedness is always a guarantee of peace," so they try their best to advocate expanding and strengthening their own military equipment. Their views on the Franco-Soviet alliance are not very agreeable. Their opinion is that in 1914, the Russian army was defeated by Hindenburg, and from the 1917 revolution to the present, "the quality of the army has not seen much progress. They are not yet fully satisfied with the operation of agricultural machinery, and the control of railways has not yet been completed. The 'human' elements indispensable for building an air force are also not very well equipped. They also believe that 'Russians are innately unsuitable for aviation,' even if they have more than 3,000 aircraft, the actual combat effectiveness is to be discounted. However, today's France, its own strength, cannot completely maintain the status quo, that is, barely support, it has to rely on the Soviet Union, and expand its strength, in order to maintain its advantage over Germany. (May 15th, Berlin)

Page 8

Zhangbei Incident: Agreement Reached on Resolution Path, Matsui Returns to Tianjin from Changchun, Men Zhizhong Goes to Chahar to Meet Song 74

Beiping Correspondence: Since the so-called Hebei issue and the Zhangbei incident successively occurred, rumors have been rampant. Regarding the Zhangbei incident, Matsui Gennosuke, the Japanese military liaison officer stationed in Zhangjiakou, and Qin Dechun, the Director of Civil Affairs of the Chahar Provincial Government, have repeatedly negotiated in Zhangjiakou, Beiping, Tianjin, and other places. Although the content is not easy to hear, the demands made by the Japanese side can only be regarded as consultations on opinions before obtaining the consent of the Japanese Kwantung Army. Therefore, after Matsui consulted with Qin Dechun in Tianjin, he went to Changchun on the 16th to report the progress of the consultation in Tianjin to the leaders of the Japanese Kwantung Army and offer resolution opinions. The Japanese Kwantung Army then telegraphed Sakai Takashi, the Chief of Staff of the Japanese Army stationed in Tianjin, to fly to Changchun on the 17th to participate in the meeting. On the 18th, according to a Changchun telegram received from related parties, the Japanese Kwantung Army's response to the Zhangbei incident has been decided to be the responsibility of Matsui, to negotiate and resolve directly with the Chahar provincial authorities according to the nature of the local incident. Matsui also flew back to Tianjin on the 18th, reported the progress of the Changchun meeting to Doihara, who was staying in Tianjin, and then continued to negotiate with Qin Dechun, the Director of Civil Affairs of Chahar, to seek a final solution. In the afternoon of the same day, at 4:00 PM, the Tianjin Japanese Garrison Headquarters specially convened an important meeting to discuss everything. Qin Dechun was also invited to attend temporarily.

It was not until 6:00 PM that it ended. Qin and Matsui will take the same car to Beiping tomorrow (the 19th) and return to Zhangjiakou. Continued report: Regarding the Zhangbei issue, the Chinese and Japanese sides negotiated in Tianjin for several days. The initial proposed solution was met with objections from the Kwantung Army. Iwai, Matsui, and Sakai requested instructions from the Kwantung Army Headquarters and left Tianjin for Changchun at noon on the 17th. He Yingqin, the Acting Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, telegraphed the Beiping Military Affairs Commission from Nanjing on the 17th, inquiring about the latest developments in the Chahar negotiations. The Military Affairs Commission replied in detail that evening, and the central government's response to the case and the progress of the Chahar provincial representatives' negotiations in Tianjin were also presented in detail by Men Zhizhong, the Standing Committee Member of the Military Affairs Commission, Yang Zhennan, the Secretary-General of the 29th Army, and Feng Zhi'an, the Commander of the 137th Division, who took the Ping-Sui train to Zhangjiakou this morning (the 18th) at 8:00 AM to report to Song Zheyuan, the Chairman of Chahar, in detail, and to coordinate with Song Zheyuan on the new handling methods of Chahar's military and political affairs. Generally speaking, the Zhangbei incident can be resolved after Matsui and Qin Dechun return to Zhangjiakou to continue negotiations. (The 18th)

Southern Anhui Rapeseed Export: Short-Term Tax of 15/1000 Levied Specifically for Wuhu Municipal Construction Expenses 75

Wuhu Correspondence: Among the agricultural products of Southern Anhui, rice is the largest, and among the miscellaneous grains, rapeseed occupies the largest share. Each year, after the oil mills in various counties have used their fill, 300,000 to 400,000 piculs are collected in Wuhu for export. The only market is in the eastern neighbor. Due to diplomatic relations over the years, every time the new rapeseed enters the market, there is a trend of strikes and bans. However, due to overproduction, economic policies for farmers and merchants, and other reasons, the result is often a discretionary tax levy, and exports continue as usual. Japanese merchants also send people to Wuhu to sit and collect, as a customary practice. This year, the rapeseed harvest in various counties in Southern Anhui is particularly abundant. At this time of rural economic panic, finding a way out is even more urgent. After much hesitation, it was decided to continue the methods of the past two years, levying a public welfare donation on rapeseed exports, as a special fund for Wuhu local construction. This donation can collect 30,000 to 40,000 yuan each time. The expansion and construction of major roads such as Zhongshan Road Second Street in Wuhu all rely on this to be completed. Currently, the provincial government is preparing for the construction of Greater Wuhu, which requires even more expenses. The proposal to continue levying rapeseed export donations is welcomed by all parties. After Lou Daoxin, the Director of the Wuhu Public Works Bureau, telegraphed suggestions to both the Provincial Finance and Construction Departments, Yang and Liu, the two directors, consulted and agreed that rapeseed is a short-term business, and a short-term business tax should be levied. In order to take into account the undertakings that should be handled in Wuhu's municipal administration, the tax rate should be appropriately increased. After being presented to the provincial government for a meeting, it was decided to handle as proposed, and both the Finance and Construction Departments were ordered to jointly entrust the Wuhu Local Tax Bureau to collect the tax according to the agreed tax rate, and to appoint Lou Daoxin, the Director of the Wuhu Public Works Bureau, to establish an office to handle rapeseed export registration matters. After this provincial order arrived in Wuhu, the Local Tax Bureau and the Public Works Bureau actively prepared to start collecting, and Japanese merchants and grain merchants also began to take action. (The 18th)

Japanese Merchant Ship Causes Trouble in Changde, Hunan: Rapid Speed Causes Sinking of Grain Boat, Headquarters Telegraphed Provincial Government for Negotiations 76

Changsha Correspondence: Japanese Dyson Chang Company merchant ships sailing on inland rivers often cause incidents. Recently, the company's Daji ship was sailing downstream in Changde. Due to its rapid speed, it sank a grain boat of the First Route Headquarters of the Bandit Suppression Army, containing 380 piculs of grain. Five boatmen, men and women, all drowned. Fortunately, nearby rowing boats were able to rescue them, preventing fatalities. The First Route Headquarters believes that the occurrence of this matter will affect the future of military food supplies. Yesterday, they telegraphed the Hunan Provincial Government, requesting serious negotiations with the Japanese Consul stationed in Hunan, ordering the Dyson Chang Company to compensate, in order to protect military food supplies. The original telegram is as follows: "According to the report of our headquarters' military grain escort officer, Huang Mingzhi Xiao Guigu, on the 9th of this month, we set sail at 9:30 AM on the 8th and arrived at Dalian Port at 1:30 AM on the 9th. We encountered the Dyson Chang Company's Daji ship, sailing downstream from Changde at high speed, which directly crashed and sank one of our civilian boats containing 380 piculs of grain. There were five boatmen, men and women, on board, all of whom drowned. There were many rowing boats in the area, and they were able to rescue them, preventing fatalities. I ordered the Daji ship that caused the accident to be escorted to Changde. In addition to requesting Chief Hu to investigate and compensate, I am reporting the facts to your attention and requesting that you seriously negotiate with the company and order them to compensate in full for the loss, in order to protect the military food supplies. I await your orders." The report from Hu, the resident Chief of the Administration Office of our headquarters in Changde, states that Huang Mingzhi arrived in Changde today with the grain, and according to him, at 1:00 AM last night, a grain boat was sunk by the Dyson Chang Daji ship in the Dayun Port of Yuanjiang, losing 380 piculs. The Daji ship has been detained. Please instruct on how to handle this situation. Therefore, in addition to telegraphing a reply, I have found that the ship belongs to a Japanese merchant, and I am hereby telegraphing you to request that you investigate and seriously negotiate with the Japanese Consul and order the company to compensate in full for the loss, in order to protect the military food supplies, and please reply for our information. Commander-in-Chief He Jian kowtows with the seal of sincerity."

Silkworm Industry in Jiangsu Province This Spring: Striving to Reduce Costs and Improve Quality, Hoping for Government and Social Cooperation to Control the Silk Industry 77

Zhenjiang News: The Jiangsu Construction Department, noting that Jiangsu Province has vast areas suitable for mulberry cultivation on both sides of the Yangtze River, and that farmers in the counties along the Grand Canal in southern Jiangsu rely on sericulture as an important sideline, with the money flowing into rural areas each year, even with today's extremely low cocoon prices, still reaching more than 10 million yuan, which is of great importance to the national economy and people's livelihood. In recent years, silk stocks have been sluggish and silver prices have soared, leading to a sharp drop in silk prices and economic hardship for farmers and merchants. To seek salvation, it is hoped that all related industries (breeders, silkworm farmers, cocoon merchants, silk merchants) can, under the current silk prices, strive to reduce costs and improve quality, struggle hard, support each other, and engage in rational management in order to survive. Therefore, the level of seed prices and cocoon prices should be related to the rise and fall of silk prices, and should never exceed this limit to obtain extra benefits. Otherwise, not only will they not be able to survive, but they will also increase the destruction of the entire silk industry. The reason is clear. The Jiangsu Construction Department, in view of this, organized the Sericulture Improvement Management Committee in the spring of the 23rd year, bringing together sericulture industry personnel to discuss and implement the control and management of the sericulture industry, in order to achieve harmony and connection among related industries. In the past year, the universal implementation of silkworm rearing guidance, the promotion and encouragement of high-yield varieties, the gradual normalization of cocoon brokerage operations, and the annual reduction of baking and reeling losses have all achieved significant results. The following is a record of the operations during the spring silkworm season this year.

Silkworm Seed Production

This year's spring seed, for the convenience of seed sales, various seed farms were allowed to buy and sell freely at the prescribed price (40 cents per sheet), and the government subsidized each sheet by 20 to 40 cents (this year, in order to encourage high-yield varieties, in addition to the Guizhu, Xin Gui, and Hua Wu Hua Liu varieties of mixed breeding, which are subsidized by the government at 20 cents per sheet, the Han Gui and Hua Wu Hua Liu varieties of mixed breeding are subsidized at 25 cents per sheet, the Xi Qiao Xi Qia and Hua Wu Hua Liu varieties of mixed breeding are subsidized at 30 cents per sheet, and the Hua Gui and Hua Liu varieties of mixed breeding are subsidized at 40 cents per sheet). The production volume in Jiangsu Province is estimated to be more than 800,000 sheets in spring and more than 400,000 sheets in autumn. Originally, it was stipulated that the spring production should be kept in the province and the autumn production should be exported. However, when the Jiangsu Construction Department inspected the silkworm seeds, it was discovered that various seed farms had failed to comply with the regulations and, without approval, had exported part of the spring production to Zhejiang Province, resulting in exports to Zhejiang reaching 600,000 sheets, leaving only 600,000 sheets in Jiangsu, which was difficult to meet the demand. The Jiangsu Construction Department immediately telegraphed various exporting farms and the Zhejiang Construction Department to withhold the seeds. However, because Zhejiang Province was hatching earlier and had a great need for seeds, part of them had already been shipped out, and because Zhejiang Province had reached an agreement with various seed farms in advance, after several consultations, only 10,000 sheets were withheld. This is the main reason for the shortage of spring seeds this year. In mid-April, the weather was sunny and the mulberry trees grew better, and the interest of silkworm farmers in sericulture increased greatly. In addition, due to the sudden warm weather in early spring, many local seeds hatched due to improper protection, and the need for improved seeds increased. The sales of these 631,800 sheets of silkworm seeds were not controlled and managed by the government, but entrusted to seed vendors by various farms, making it difficult to achieve proper distribution. Seed vendors manipulated the market, raised prices, and exploited farmers, which is deeply hateful. In order to relieve silkworm farmers and suppress price increases, the government had no choice but to order more than 31,000 sheets of silkworm seeds from Japan and transport them to various regions for sale to adjust the market. However, this move was unfavorable to seed vendors, resulting in the destruction of silkworm seed sales points on May 2. Although the incident was quickly quelled, the estimated shortage of silkworm seeds in the province still reached about 50,000 sheets). In order to improve the quality of silkworm cocoons, the Sericulture Improvement Management Committee stipulated high-yield and robust varieties and designated breeding areas, in order to unify the quality of fresh cocoons and reduce baking and reeling losses. The stipulated varieties are first and second generation hybrids, with the first generation being Guizhu, Xin Gui, Han Gui, Hua Gui, Xi Qiao Xi Qia, and the second generation being Hua Wu Hua Liu, and strictly prohibiting the breeding of pure varieties and other varieties.

Silkworm Rearing Guidance

This spring, Jiangsu Province has 2 centers in Wuxi and Jintan, and 13 improved areas in Wujin, Jiangyin, Yixing, Liyang, Danyang, Wuxian, Wujiang, Zhenjiang, Jurong, Yangzhou, Jiangdu, Changshu, and Jingjiang, all of which adopt a central guidance system. Based on the distribution of silkworm farmers in each county under the area office, central guidance stations are established to handle silkworm farmer surveys, disinfection of silkworm rooms and tools, joint hatching, joint breeding of young silkworms, and organization of sericulture cooperatives. In the central guidance area, silkworm rearing guidance stations are set up to guide silkworm farmers in silkworm rearing and mulberry planting, in order to improve silkworm rearing technology and rationalize management. The province has a total of 38 central guidance stations and 268 guidance stations.

Cocoon Brokerage Control

Since Jiangsu Province opened cocoon brokerages in the 17th year, the number of stoves has greatly increased, and the amount of fresh cocoons cannot correspond to the number of baking stoves, resulting in increased cocoon collection costs. Since the spring of the 23rd year, cocoon brokerage control has been implemented, so that cocoon brokerages can operate in an orderly manner, save unnecessary expenses, improve baking technology and cocoon collection organization, in order to reduce dry cocoon costs and improve quality.

In the spring cocoon season this year, in order to thoroughly implement cocoon brokerage control, the first step is to rectify cocoon brokerages. For all cocoon brokerages in the model area and improved area, the area will inspect the cocoon licenses. Those with licenses but no stoves will have their cocoon licenses revoked, and those with stoves but no licenses will have their stoves demolished. Cocoon brokerages with only single stoves of 4x4 or less, except for those that are indeed self-used stoves of cooperatives, will have their cocoon licenses revoked and the license fees will be refunded by the association according to their effective term. Half a month before the cocoon brokerages open, each area will estimate the amount of fresh cocoons produced in the current season, formulate the number of stoves of cocoon brokerages that are allowed to open, and submit them to the Sericulture Improvement Management Committee for approval and promulgation. After the approved number of stoves is promulgated, the registration of cocoon collectors will begin. All qualified cocoon brokerages can recruit cocoon collectors and register with each area to open and collect cocoons. Those who are not registered will not be allowed to open. If the number of registered stoves has reached the approved number of stoves, the registration will be closed. However, qualified firms that have not been able to register cocoon collectors in this session will still have the right to register and collect cocoons in the next session. In order to eliminate the malpractices of cocoon collection, it is strictly forbidden to use old scales, collect cocoons at night, and crack down on bad habits such as cocoon vendors, scalpers, and the use of small foreign copper coins to protect the interests of silkworm farmers.

Results of Operations

It is estimated that the province will produce about 300,000 piculs of fresh cocoons this spring. The average price of improved seed cocoons is 20 yuan per picul. The amount of cocoons collected from each improved seed by guided silkworm farmers ranges from 30 jin to more than 50 jin per sheet, with baking losses ranging from 300 jin to 270 jin, and reeling losses ranging from 410 jin to 360 jin. Compared with last year, there has been significant progress. This is due to the improvement of silkworm seeds, the standardization of varieties, and the improvement of silkworm rearing technology. (Note) Last year, the amount of cocoons collected from each improved seed was about 30 jin to 40 jin, with baking losses ranging from 300 jin to 280 jin, and reeling losses ranging from 450 jin to 400 jin. Now, if each silkworm farmer raises two sheets of improved seeds, they can collect about 80 jin of fresh cocoons, worth 16 yuan. After deducting the silkworm seed price of 80 cents and the miscellaneous expenses required for silkworm rearing of about 1.2 yuan, there is still a profit of 14 yuan. Although the cocoon price is low, the farmers in Jiangsu Province after the disaster have benefited greatly from this income. This can be proven by the fact that the agricultural warehouses in various counties after the cocoon market are redeeming the items they had pledged. Furthermore, according to the productivity of mulberry gardens in Jiangsu Province in recent years, each mu of mulberry garden can produce enough mulberry leaves to feed two sheets of improved seeds. According to the above calculation, the input per mu of mulberry garden is 14 yuan (the silkworm rearing time is short, and the profit comes from labor, so the silkworm rearing labor costs can be ignored). The income is not yet included. If compared with rice fields and cotton fields, it may not be much less. Therefore, sericulture is a good sideline that nourishes the countryside. In the future, if we can work hard to improve and standardize silkworm varieties, in order to reduce baking and reeling losses, then even if silk prices remain the same, cocoon prices can still rise accordingly. This is to be hoped for through the cooperation of the government and society to promote the success of sericulture control.

Cuttlefish Reproduction Experiment at the Zhejiang Aquatic Products Experiment Station – Experiment Location in Shengshan – 78

Dinghai Correspondence: Regarding the cuttlefish netting problem, the Zhejiang Aquatic Products Experiment Station, after receiving orders to study it, immediately consulted with the Jiangsu Provincial Aquatic Products School and agreed on a cooperative approach. They jointly hired fishermen, equipped fishing boats and fishing gear, and borrowed the site of the Jiangsu Provincial Fisheries Experiment Station in Shengshan as a research experiment location. They also sent personnel to live in Shengshan for a long time to conduct experiments. The Zhejiang station is responsible for the cuttlefish life history and reproduction experiments. The reproduction experiment uses tree branches, bamboo branches, rice straw, and other materials to sink to the seabed as objects for cuttlefish eggs to attach to, which is a good way to remedy overfishing. Chen Tongbai, the head of the station, took the Chaoyang ship to Shengshan on the 13th of this month to observe the reproduction experiment and guide the research methods of cuttlefish occurrence. He returned to Dinghai on the evening of the 16th. According to him, the results of the reproduction experiment are quite good. He estimates that if the government can use 1,000 yuan per year for reproduction, it can cultivate about 200 million eggs. With a survival rate of one-tenth, about 20 million adult cuttlefish can be obtained, and each hundred worth one yuan, then the total value is 200,000. This reproduction method is well worth trying. Director Chen also accompanied the fishing boats out to sea to observe netting and cage fishing methods. According to him, this year's first two waters of cuttlefish are not very abundant, and after the third water, there are almost no catches to be had. Although there are no statistics to illustrate, it can also be seen that the reduction of cuttlefish is quite obvious. Remedial measures are really unavoidable. (The 17th)

All special agents stationed in Songjiang have been replaced by others sent from Songjiang.

Shen Xiyuan Suddenly Flees and Attempts Suicide 82

Shen Xiyuan, the accountant of Huizhong Hotel, was 34 years old. He had an affair with a woman named Liu Caizhen, and they had a child. Liu repeatedly asked Shen to divorce his original wife and then formally marry her. Shen’s original wife, Cheng, was unwilling to agree, and they already had two sons and four daughters. Shen and Cheng had a very close relationship on weekdays. Therefore, Shen had no way to resolve this situation. Liu had arranged to marry Shen at the Suzhou Hotel today (the 19th). Liu’s relatives and friends had all arrived to offer their congratulations. Unexpectedly, both Shen and Liu suddenly disappeared temporarily. It was later discovered that Shen had attempted suicide by eating raw opium at the Shijia Hotel in Mudu. He was discovered by the tea attendant but was not dead. Liu was found at her sister’s place. Her sister is Tan Zhonghui, the head of the Secretariat of the Central Bank of Shanghai.

Wuxi: Preparing to Form a Disaster Prevention Committee 83

After last year’s early drought, due to scarce rainfall this year, the signs of another drought are emerging. The County Party Headquarters believes that water conservancy in the county has not been repaired in recent years, and disasters have occurred repeatedly. It is urgent to organize a disaster prevention committee to coordinate disaster prevention work. This was submitted to the 15th Party-Government Talks yesterday and resolved. The Disaster Prevention Committee is to be formed by the County Party Headquarters, County Government, Construction Bureau, Public Security Bureau, Land Bureau, Farmers Bank, Sericulture Experiment Station, County Chamber of Commerce, County Property Office, and district chiefs from each district, to coordinate disaster prevention work. At the same time, it was also decided to organize a Party-Government-Military-Education-Sports Promotion Association in accordance with provincial orders.

Water Patrol Team Captures Six Robbers 84

Zhou Rongchun and Zhou Fengdi, fishermen from this county, went to Hengjing in the Fifth District to fish. Unexpectedly, they were robbed by thieves in the middle of the night the day before yesterday, and were tied up with ropes, suffering a total loss of more than 300 yuan. The next day, when Zhou Rongchun and Zhou Fengdi were sailing their boat near Xicang River to fish, eight awning boats suddenly approached. Rongchun, suspicious, immediately stopped fishing and carefully observed. He recognized two of the boatmen, Mian Ma (pockmarked face) and Diao Yan (slanted eyes), as the robbers from the previous night. They immediately rushed to the water patrol team stationed at Doumenbang to request a team to investigate and arrest them. Upon receiving the report, Police Chief Cai immediately led six patrol boats in two directions to pursue and arrest them. They were apprehended at Xicang Town and the eight awning boats were seized. Six robbers, Jiang Guifu (Mian Ma), Jiang Changyin (Diao Yan), and suspects Pan Zhuyou, Jiang Changshou, Jiang Guanghe, and Li Guixiang, were arrested on the spot. Police Chief Cai escorted them to the Shuixian Temple team headquarters in Nanmen for interrogation. Later, 19 family members of the suspects, Li Qiaoying, Jiang Tushi, Jiang Kou Nv, and Li Lushi, followed them to the front of the water patrol team, crying loudly and making noise to the team members. Captain Zhang Rongxing of the team had no choice but to prepare a document and send them, along with the captured bandits and the victims Zhou Rongchun and Zhou Fengdi, to the County Public Security Bureau for transfer to the County Government for interrogation.

The County Public Security Bureau Supervision Department dispatched police officers to arrest gamblers at You Fuquan's house at No. 57 Houzhongzheng Road the day before yesterday. At that time, Guo Fu, a partner in a boarding house in Changkang Lane, was there to collect a three-yuan meal debt. He was watching from the side when the police arrived. Panicked, he jumped from the second floor, intending to escape. Unexpectedly, he landed on the water tank below, causing severe injuries to his waist and back. The police officers took six male and female gamblers to the bureau for punishment. Guo was sent to the Brothers Hospital for treatment, but his internal organs were ruptured. He died yesterday morning around 1:00 a.m. Xi Zhiliang, the head of Tian San Tu, reported to the local branch hospital for an autopsy. Guo was from Jiangyin. His family members have heard the news and are coming to Wuxi to handle everything.

Zhenjiang: Female Residents of Relief Home Seek Marriage 87

The Jiangsu Provincial Relief Home once openly advertised for marriage partners in order to improve the marriage prospects of the female residents of the relief home, achieving satisfactory results. Now that the second open recruitment period is approaching, the home has selected 26 female residents, including Chen Jinzhi, who have received training in housework, handicrafts, education, and other courses, as well as personal cultivation, and who are of excellent character and scholarship and are capable of managing a household, for open recruitment of marriage partners. Among the female residents seeking marriage partners, one-third have a secondary or elementary education level, and others have special skills in handicrafts. Yangzhou: Dredging the Shahe River to Promote the Market 88

Executive Committee Member Wang Bailing believes that the abolition of sail transport at Twelve Forts has had a huge impact on the Yangzhou city market. He has jointly requested the dredging of the Shahe River outside Dongguan City with Miao Qiujie, the Salt Transport Envoy of Lianghuai, and Jin Xiangsheng, the Deputy Salt Transport Envoy of Huainan, based on the proposal of local resident Hu Zhi, so that people and goods between Jiangsu, Anhui, Shanghai, and Suzhou can be transported here, directly revitalizing Yangzhou's industry and commerce, and indirectly transferring the livelihoods of the former workers of the Twelve Forts salt affairs. It is heard that the dredging fee of the river and all expenses for converting the old earth dam into a ship lock will require at least 520,000 yuan. This amount may be approved by the Ministry of Finance and the National Economic Commission, allowing it to be withdrawn from the national treasury. It is now learned that Committee Member Wang and others have specially drawn up maps and engineering plans and sent letters to various water conservancy experts and local officials and gentry, soliciting opinions. In addition, the Ten Forts Salt Maintenance Association previously strongly advocated for wheel-sail transport and requested a delay in the implementation of the sail reduction measures. The Ministry of Finance did not approve it, and they recently submitted another appeal, while also delegating representatives Duan Zhizhou and Wu Bingcheng to submit reports to the Provincial Government, the Department of Civil Affairs, the Provincial Federation of Commerce, the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, the Zhenjiang Shipping Association, and other organizations, requesting unanimous assistance in forwarding the request to the Ministry of Finance to postpone the sail reduction measures until after the implementation of the new salt law, and to approve the wheel-sail transport agreement, so that hundreds of millions of fort workers can be revived and their livelihoods maintained.

Jiaxing: National Goods Company Closes for Inventory 95

The Jiaxing China National Goods Company on Jilu Road in the north of Jiaxing, which opened in December last year, happened to coincide with years of famine and economic collapse. The buying power of the people was weak. Although the managers tried their best to operate it, the turnover decreased day by day, and it could not be maintained. More than 30 employees of the company believed that although the company's sudden closure was unavoidable, it was difficult to find another job at this time. Haimen: Three Factory Employees Assault Party Committee Member 96

Dasheng Third Factory in Changle Town, Third District, experienced a strike on the 7th of this month due to layoffs and wage reductions. Party and government agencies sent people to persuade them repeatedly, but they still did not resume work. At 10:00 a.m. on the 17th, Shi Yuwen, a member of the County Party Committee and instructor of the Third Factory Trade Union, went to the Third Factory and gathered workers in the old drill ground for instructions and to solicit opinions from the workers. Several employees of the Third Factory mingled among the workers to gather information. Fearing that there would be misunderstandings between the staff and workers, Shi ordered them to withdraw to avoid disputes. After the instructions were completed, the workers gradually dispersed. Suddenly, more than 70 employees of the factory crowded around, shouting "Down with Shi Yuwen" and surrounded and attacked Shi. Shi bravely broke through the encirclement and fled north. The employees continued to chase after him. Seeing the dangerous situation, Shi leaped across two creeks and hid in the reeds for an hour. Later, he fled to the home of a villager named Wu, disguised as a farmer, and circled to the county seat from Wu's town around 3:00 p.m., finally escaping safely. The County Party Committee Standing Committee member Xiao requested County Magistrate Chen to verify the injuries and punish the perpetrators severely. On the morning of the 18th, County Magistrate Chen sent the Deputy Commander of the Security Brigade, He Keqian, to thoroughly investigate the truth of the incident for prosecution.

Letter 97

To the Editor, I am writing to you regarding the Songjiang correspondence published in your newspaper on June 15th, "Another Kidnapping Case in Fengjing." It stated that Qian Qichang, a farmer in Fanbang Township, Fengjing, at the intersection of Songjiang and Qingpu, was robbed the night before last by more than 20 bandits speaking with a Chaohu accent, each carrying sharp weapons. They kidnapped Qian Qichang's eight-month-old son and a worker, along with all the small boats, and so on. Upon investigation, the county village and Miao mentioned in the report do not exactly match the facts. It has been found that I live in Sanhe Village, Fifth Bao, Xin Town, Third District, Qingpu County. At about 12:00 a.m. on the night of the 11th of this month, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came, speaking in mixed accents and holding guns. They broke into my house and went straight into the workers' bedroom, tying up six workers including Cai Shengtang, arbitrarily beating them, and forcing Cai Shengtang to lead them to my wife Qi Shen's bedroom. They kidnapped my wife and my eight-month-old child Haoran, along with the worker Cai Shengtang. The bandits drove an awning boat halfway and released my wife Qi Shen and Cai Shengtang one after another, ordering them to prepare money to redeem my eight-month-old son Haoran. When they opened the boat, they also robbed one of my agricultural boats. Fortunately, I stayed in the new Shangzhen Town and was not affected. I am now afraid of misunderstanding and request correction. Please investigate accordingly. I am, sincerely, Qi Qichang of Sanhe, June 17th.
