Local News

Domestic Goods Production and Sales Greatly Increased, Attention to Sales in Border Areas, Develop Overseas Markets 98

Central News Agency reports that domestic goods have been promoted and used by all sectors in recent years, and both production and sales have greatly increased. The future of the industry is very bright. It is now known that the industry is paying attention to sales in the border provinces and regions on the one hand, and is considering the development of overseas markets on the other hand in order to actively promote sodium. The Central News Agency reporter learned the details from the domestic goods industry as follows:

Suitable for Production and Sales Supply and Demand

In the past, domestic goods manufacturers only sought low costs and easy sales for the production of goods, resulting in unsustainable materials and loss of faith among buyers, which made foreign goods sell well in the market. In recent years, they have gradually considered the selection of high-quality materials and strived for cleanliness. Therefore, there has been a gradual improvement in recent years, but shoddy products have not yet disappeared. It is now known that in order to increase the faith of buyers of domestic goods, leaders in the industry have decided that the industry will supervise and urge each other on the quality of outgoing goods. At the same time, the output will also be controlled to make the supply and demand suitable to avoid the accumulation of inventory and increased costs.

Agreed on Methods for Promotion

Regarding sales, we are currently discussing how to increase sales day by day. There are various methods. The current methods used include (1) uniting with various guest gangs to promote goods to the mainland; (2) organizing domestic goods promotion groups to go to the mainland for exhibitions to make the public understand the difference between domestic goods and foreign goods, and the price and quality of domestic goods (3) setting up domestic goods companies in larger cities in the mainland to promote sales, etc. Other sales methods are still under discussion and progress, so that compatriots across the country can purchase and use domestic goods and restore interests.

Mainland People Are Happy to Purchase

Now, people in various places are increasingly aware of the low price and high quality of domestic goods, which are better than imported goods, so the purchase of old goods is also gradually increasing. As for the border provinces and regions, foreign goods are sold everywhere in recent years due to the dumping of foreign goods in the mainland. Since the domestic goods promotion groups went to exhibit, the public's willingness to purchase domestic goods in the area has increased significantly. Therefore, the business communities in major cities in Gansu, Shaanxi, Shanxi, Sichuan, Yunnan, and other provinces have contacted the domestic goods industry in this port to negotiate methods of promoting domestic goods, and several places have signed distribution contracts.

Actively Promoting Sales Overseas

The domestic goods industry has also been actively promoting overseas sales in recent years. For example, in Southeast Asia, last year, Englishman Mr. Speaker purchased a large batch of domestic goods in Shanghai and transported them to Southeast Asia by special ship for promotion. Overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia have expressed their welcome. Following him, there were other Englishmen, Smith, etc., who were able to obtain huge profits. However, the high import taxes in various places have a considerable impact. Among the domestic goods industry, the overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia have welcomed domestic goods, so they will discuss continuing to transport and sell them.

Industry and Commerce Request Relief, Amounting to More Than 30 Million, Collateral Must Be Subject to Strict Review by the Loan Association, After Passing the Review, It Will Be Lent by the Silver and Money Industry 99

Xin Xin She reports that the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Committee's articles of association and detailed rules of procedure have been discussed in several meetings, and each committee member has submitted opinions in writing to the chairman, Cai Zengji, for summarizing and discussion. It is now scheduled to hold the fourth meeting at the Guohuo Bank office at 4:00 p.m. on the 21st. After the meeting, it will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation. Guohuo Bank has allocated a large room on the second floor of the bank as the association's office, and the interior has also been arranged. Industrial and commercial enterprises in this city requesting loans have been registered by organizations such as the Zhonghua Guohuo Maintenance Association, the Zhonghua Guohuo Factory Federation, the Machine-made Guohuo Factory Federation, and the Shanghai Citizens Advocating Guohuo Association. The forms filled out by various industrial and commercial enterprises are collected by each organization and sent to the Advocating Guohuo Datongmeng Committee, and then transferred to the Loan Committee for review. Once the review is passed by the committee, the silver and money industry will be notified to implement the loan. The amount of loans requested by various industrial and commercial enterprises to various Guohuo organizations in recent days has reached more than 30 million yuan.

Relying on Foreign Goods for Clothing, Food, Housing, and Transportation; Annual Need Exceeds 400 Million Yuan; Imports Occupy Over 60 Million Gold Units in Five Months; The Only Remedy is for Compatriots to Advocate Using Domestic Products 103

According to a Xin Xin News Agency report, Wang Boyan, a specialist at the International Trade Bureau's statistics department, told a Xin Xin News Agency reporter that Shanghai's foreign trade reaches between twenty and thirty million customs gold units per month. Imports exceed exports by over ten million gold units per month, making it the largest import surplus port in the country. In the first five months of this year, its import value reached 145,077,712 gold units, and its export value reached 105,442,648 gold units, resulting in a huge import surplus of over 39,630,000 gold units. An analysis of the nature of the imports reveals that clothing, food, housing, and transportation items constitute the largest proportion, followed by luxury goods, and then production goods. In the past five months, Shanghai's reliance on foreign goods for clothing, food, housing, and transportation amounted to over 63,630,000 gold units. The breakdown is as follows:

Clothing: Cotton goods 2,874,134, cotton 11,771,081, wool products 4,222,112, silk goods 1,449,980, hemp goods 1,136,348, cotton yarn 453,742, leather goods 486,369, totaling 22,393,766 gold units.

Food: Sugar 2,118,185, rice 11,332,609, flour 61,779, grains 28,704, seafood 1,404,615, meat products, etc. 1,686,970, totaling 16,632,362 gold units.

Housing: Construction hardware 14,045,178, timber 5,485,452, stone and clay 7,511,099, glass 378,594, totaling 20,370,323 gold units.

Transportation: Gasoline 2,479,607, automobiles 1,703,135, bicycles 17,721, other vehicles 33,474, totaling 4,233,937 gold units.

The above four items total 63,630,388 gold units, accounting for 43.8% of Shanghai's total imports in the past five months. It is worth noting that in our country, which is founded on agriculture, we should not have to rely on foreigners for clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Of the above items, only construction hardware and gasoline have to be imported because the domestic steel industry is not well-developed and gasoline cannot be refined. The remaining goods can all be self-sufficient. Yet, we must rely on foreigners, spending hundreds of millions of customs gold units annually, equivalent to over 400 million yuan (national currency), to exchange for essential materials such as clothing, food, housing, and transportation. How can we prevent the bankruptcy of rural areas? The remedy should first focus on advocating the use of domestic products for clothing, food, housing, and transportation.

Tax Bureau Holds Today; Head of the Stamp and Tobacco Bureau Meeting; Eleven Have Already Reported Yesterday 104

The Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau, in order to rectify the revenue from stamp, tobacco, and alcohol taxes, has scheduled a meeting of the heads of stamp tax bureaus from ten provinces, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Henan, Fujian, Shandong, Hebei, and Hunan, for 9:00 AM today.

Two-Day Meeting

The main topic of this meeting, convened by the Tax Bureau with the deputy and senior bureau chiefs of stamp, tobacco, and alcohol taxes from various provinces, is to rectify the revenue from stamp, tobacco, and alcohol taxes. According to the reports from various bureaus for this year, as of the end of March, only one or two of the more than ten provinces were able to collect and remit funds in accordance with the quota stipulated by the Ministry of Finance. Some provinces even reported shortfalls, remitting only 30% to 40%. Therefore, it is urgent to change course and strive to remedy the situation. It is said that the meeting will last for two days.

Minsheng Industrial Company; Issuing Company Bonds I; Business Expansion Scheduled to Begin on July 1; Underwritten by Eight Banks, Including Jincheng and China 107

According to a Xin Sheng News Agency report, Minsheng Industrial Co., Ltd. purchased six ships, including Yijiang, Yixing, Qitai, Yian, Yichang, and Xietan, from the American company Jiejiang for 450,000 yuan (national currency). The company also purchased He Aiti's Qichun of Jiejiang. All of them have been successively received in Shanghai and Chongqing, and their names have been changed and added to ten routes, including Tonghe, Jarong, Fuwan, Shenyi, Yushen. Yuhe, Yufu, Yuyi and Luhan. It is understood that the company originally had 30 ships, including Minzu and Minquan, as well as tugboats Minli, Minli, and storage ships Minle. Together with the seven newly purchased ships, there are more than 40 ships in total, mainly operating in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River.

Issuing Company Bonds: The company has a capital of one million yuan (national currency), with its head office in Chongqing and branches and agencies in various ports along the Yangtze River. General Manager Lu Zuofu plans to issue company bonds worth one million yuan (national currency) to expand the business and has contacted Jincheng, China, Jiaotong, Zhongnan, Shanghai, Juxingcheng, Chuankang Zhiye, and Sichuan Meifeng banks to handle the underwriting. The above banks all agree that the company bonds issued by the company are indeed for business expansion. Now, the company bond has been approved by the shareholders' meeting and is scheduled to be issued on July 1. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency inquired from Minsheng Company yesterday that the company bond underwriting matters have been negotiated and an underwriting contract has been signed. Jincheng Bank will underwrite 400,000 yuan, Bank of China 200,000 yuan, Jiaotong and Zhongnan Banks 100,000 yuan each, and Shanghai, Juxingcheng, Sichuan Meifeng, and Chuankang Zhiye Banks 50,000 yuan each. It is stipulated that the full amount must be paid when the company bond is issued on July 1.

Organizing a Banking Syndicate: The eight banks, including Jincheng Bank, that underwrite the company bonds, have formed an underwriting syndicate, which is named "Representative Committee of Bondholders of Minsheng Industrial Co., Ltd." Jincheng Bank is responsible for serving as the chairman of the committee and presiding over everything. The general association is located at Jincheng Bank in Shanghai, and an office is established at the Bank of China in Chongqing. It is decided that the payment will be made on July 1. The term of the company bond is eight years, and the company's property and operating income are used as collateral.

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Ningbo liner, Xinjiangtian, is reorganizing the stewards, abolishing the extra stewards of the cold water shift. However, the stewards on board still remain on the ship, refusing to leave, in order to confront the company. Seafarers Oppose Pay Cuts; Awaiting Yu's Return to Shanghai to Resolve 110

The China Merchant Ship Drivers' Federation, the China Marine Engineers' Federation, and other seafarers' organizations believe that the Shanghai Shipping Association's decision to cut the salaries of crew members of all member companies earning more than 15 yuan by 20% starting on July 1 is a matter of vital importance to the livelihood of seafarers and have opposed it. The atmosphere is very tense. It is learned that Yu Qiaqing, chairman of the Shipping Association, is scheduled to return to Shanghai from Yong today to discuss a solution. The situation is described in detail below.

Crew Members of Various Ships Await Mediation

Sanbei, Ningshao, Dada, Datong, and other shipping companies have recently requested a reduction in crew salaries from the Shipping Association to maintain operations due to the decline in shipping. The association decided that starting from July 1, the salaries of crew members earning more than 15 yuan will be reduced by 20% across the board and has requested the government to issue public bonds of 10 million yuan for relief. This has led to opposition from various seafarers' organizations, which believe that the salaries of Chinese ship crew members are already very low and far from the treatment of European and American crew members. If this is implemented, the lives of seafarers will inevitably be greatly affected. Therefore, they have jointly gathered to discuss and issued a declaration of opposition. It is learned that Yu Qiaqing, chairman of the Shipping Association, has returned to Yong to avoid birthday celebrations and has not yet come to Shanghai, so the two sides have not yet formally negotiated. There is also

Page 10

no correspondence. The crew members of various ships are currently waiting for the various seafarers' organizations to resolve the matter in accordance with the law and have no other actions for the time being.

Yu Qiaqing Returns to Shanghai This Morning

Yu Qiaqing, chairman of the Shipping Association, will be 69 years old on the 15th of this month. In order to avoid celebrations from all parties and to save expenses, he returned to his ancestral home in Yong. The issue of crew salary cuts has not been formally discussed. It is learned that Yu will return to Shanghai on the Ningxing ship this morning. Seafarers' organizations in the city are also scheduled to send representatives to the Shipping Association at 9:00 AM today to demand that the original wages be maintained in order to avoid disputes. It is also learned that the Special Party Department of the Chinese Seafarers will convene a meeting this Saturday to discuss how to deal with the matter.

Jointly Requesting Relief from the Central Government

The China Marine Engineers' Federation, the China Drivers' Federation, the Radio Officers' Welfare Association, and other seafarers' organizations have issued a declaration opposing the Chinese merchant shipping companies' crew salary cuts. In addition, organizations such as Yanying Nanshe, New Taikoo Cargo Handling Club, Beijun'an Sailor's Guild, Yanying General Agency, Nanjun'an Sailor's Charity Association, Navigation Helmsman Carpenter Mutual Aid Association, Chinese Navigation Drivers' Federation, Sanbei Hongan Cargo Handling Club, Navigation Lianyi Association, Yihe Cargo Handling Club, and Liyixuan Lodging House have jointly opposed the Shanghai Shipping Association's announcement of crew salary cuts. In addition to an urgent announcement, they have also requested the Special Party Department of the Seafarers and others to fight for the cause. Dredging Yuji Pier; Resolution to Requisition Civilian Land 115

The Yangtze River Conservancy Commission, in view of the fact that the Wusong River has been in disrepair for many years and is becoming increasingly silted up, previously submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to request the Ministry of Finance to approve the allocation of funds for dredging. However, the Yuji Pier section in West Shanghai needs to be straightened and a new channel needs to be opened, requiring the requisition of more than 300 mu of civilian land. The farmers there have repeatedly opposed it and jointly requested the city government and the Municipal Farmers' Association to provide relief in order to maintain the livelihood of the farmers. Now, the Conservancy Commission has invited relevant groups to meet and resolve the matter. Regarding the method of requisitioning civilian land, (1) the land price is negotiated and 180 yuan per mu is paid, (2) the seedling fee is 8 yuan per mu, and the mud piling part will be paid after the completion of the project, (3) the relocation compensation will be handled in accordance with the regulations of the Shanghai Land Bureau, (4) the seedling fee and land price within the new river line will be paid first, and then construction will begin, (5) if the land deed and grain string are lost, the owner will invite the map director and land security to provide written proof and declare the loss in the newspaper before they can receive the payment. Yesterday, the resolution was sent to the Pusong District Farmers' Association for implementation.

Attendees included Executive Committee members Zhao Jinqing, Du Yuesheng, Chen Heqin, Wu Weide, Cao Yunxiang, Dr. Yan Fuqing, Zhu Lide, Sun Ruihuang, Fei Wusheng, Wei Zhihua, Mrs. Helmick, and attendees including General Secretary Xu Jianping, Deputy General Secretary Chen Tiesheng, etc. Chairman Zhao Jinqing presided over the meeting according to the agenda. First, Secretary Chen Heqin read the minutes of the previous meeting, which were approved by all. Then, Accountant Sun Ruihuang reported on the economic situation of the association in the past month. General Secretary Xu Jianping reported on the association's affairs in the past month. Xu's statement was as follows: In the past month, the association has done the following in terms of general affairs: (1) The association selected Ms. Ding Yijing as a representative to attend the 5th International Conference on Family Education to discuss matters related to promoting international family education. The conference will hold its opening ceremony in Brussels, Belgium on July 31. The association has already sent an English promotional brochure to Representative Ding, and will soon send the conference proposal and China's family education papers together. (2) The National Children's Year Implementation Committee has held meetings twice in the capital. Luo Yunyan, Chen Heqin, Ding Shujing, and Guan Cuizhen (as representatives) brought many proposals prepared by the secretariat for reference when they left. (3) The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau sent a letter inviting the association to send a representative to participate in the Shanghai Children's Year Implementation Committee. Chen Tiesheng has been sent as the association's representative to participate and has been notified of the future. (4) The Tzu Yu American Association sent a letter stating that Mrs. Roberts has been selected to come to China to discuss the construction of the Nanjing Model Education Institute. (5) The 214th meeting of the Executive Yuan of the National Government has approved an annual subsidy of 80,000 yuan to the association to carry out national Tzu Yu undertakings. (6) Other, in terms of protection, the association has handled 15 cases involving children, including 4 cases of stepmothers abusing children, 2 cases of prostitute complaints, 1 case of lost children, 1 case of fathers abusing daughters, 1 case of child trafficking, and 4 cases of abandoned children. In terms of education, the association has organized the Modern Parents Monthly Editorial Committee, preparing for the publication of the Modern Parents Monthly and Children's Year special issue, and held radio broadcasts. The speakers were Ms. Yao Shuwen and Dr. Huang Huiguang. In terms of hygiene, 86 sick children from the Shanghai Women's Association Voluntary Elementary School were treated, and 324 vaccinations were given to children from the association's affiliated institutions and the Women's Association Voluntary Elementary School. The agricultural children's education centers in Zhuanqiao District and Maqiao District of Shanghai held children's health competitions on May 12 and 24 respectively. The association specially sent Dr. Liu Yide to assist in the organization. In terms of various experimental areas, the Tzu Yu Education Institute houses 75 children, 7 of whom will graduate from senior elementary school this summer. The institute will find ways to help them continue their education. The Tzu Yu Nursery houses 52 children, all of whom are from working-class families and are very grateful to the institute. The Tzu Yu Clinic treated 1,845 sick children, visited the families of sick children 84 times, held children's meetings 4 times, and provided free bathing for children 9 times. The Tzu Yu Tuberculosis Sanatorium houses 35 sick children, providing them with opportunities for reading and playing in addition to appropriate treatment. Subsequently, the Peiping People's Education Institute houses 103 children. Various handicraft industries are being actively promoted. After the report was completed, the following important proposals were approved: (1) Hire accountant Pan Xulun to audit the association's accounts for the past six months. (2) Actively build a clubhouse in Shanghai, with the original 10,000 yuan designated for construction. More large donations should be sought to complete the construction plan. (3) As for whether a certain plot of land on Qiqi Road in the French Concession, mentioned by Dr. Yan Fuqing, is suitable for building a clubhouse, the General Secretary should be instructed to inspect and study it and submit a report at the next meeting. (4) The drawings of the Nanjing Model Education Institute (drafted by engineer Li Yang'an) are generally very complete, but as to whether the scope needs to be expanded, the General Secretary should be instructed to carefully revise and supplement them. (5) The association's promotion plan proposed by the General Secretary should be submitted to the Promotion Committee for research and then reported. (6) The request of Ms. Hyde, a Westerner in Fuzhou, for assistance from the association should be submitted to the Promotion Committee for research and then reported. (7) Other matters. After the proposals were passed, the meeting was adjourned, and it was already 2:30.

International Lawyers Association, Ling Qihan Represents 122

The Lawyers Association of the Republic of China, for the International Lawyers Association General Assembly which is about to open, in addition to deciding to entrust Mr. Ling Qihan, the chargé d'affaires stationed in Belgium, to attend and participate on behalf of our country's legal community, has also sent the proposed motions to various lawyers' associations to solicit opinions, set a deadline for submission to the association, and assigned personnel to review them, and then submit them to Ling, the acting representative stationed in Belgium, to be submitted to the General Assembly for discussion at that time.

County Agricultural Loan Office Has Been Opened 123

The Shanghai County Party Department, the County Government, and the Fund Property Office, etc., considering that the agricultural season is approaching and fearing that farmers lack capital, have organized agricultural loans. They have borrowed funds from Xinhua Bank. Therefore, the Agricultural Loan Office was established and opened the previous day, with Tang Jimin as the director. Branch offices were also established in various districts, with the district chiefs concurrently serving as directors. Farmers can borrow 5 to 10 yuan, and at most 20 yuan. If the farmers are indeed without capital, they can find a guarantor to borrow from the branch offices. The monthly interest rate is 1.2%, and if it is less than a month, it is calculated by the day. The debt must be cleared within January of the 25th year.

Shanghai Mental Hospital Will Open 124

The newly built Shanghai Mental Hospital will open at the end of this month. Half of the funding is donated by the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Public Concession Engineering Bureau, and the French Concession Public Works Bureau, and half is raised by the initiator Lu Bohong. The hospital occupies 150 acres and can accommodate about 600 patients. The equipment is very complete. A part of the hospital building is allocated to teach mental illness treatment methods to the Shanghai National Medical College. Lu Bohong is the general director and Dr. Hafen is the director of the medical department. The doctors are all famous experts from China and abroad. The male and female nurses have also received special training. In the future, after its establishment, it will truly be a blessing for those suffering from mental illness.

Public Buses Overloading Passengers, Fines for Violations, Each Fine is 5 Yuan 125

The Great American Evening News reported that the Shanghai Public Concession Tram Company was found by the patrol for overloading passengers on four occasions last week and was sued in the British Consulate Police Court. It was sentenced to a fine of 15 yuan each time. The Chinese Public Bus Company was also sued for four violations. This morning (19th), Magistrate Haines opened the trial. Because the company's engineer and traffic supervisor Xu Te testified in court that a week before receiving the summons, he ordered ticket sellers to stop the bus when it was overcrowded, to summon patrol officers to reduce the number of passengers to the legal limit, and ordered ticket sellers not to collect excess fares, he was leniently sentenced to a fine of 5 yuan each time to close the case.

British National Gan Erde's Case of Crushing a Rickshaw Puller to Death with His Own Car, Fellow Villagers Formed a Victim Support Association, Planning to Petition the Municipal Government and Various Agencies 126

The British national Gan Erde's private car, number 11243, on May 8th of this year at 8:05 pm, passed in front of number 03 on Xiafei Road. The driver was not careful and overturned the rickshaw pulled by Sun Quanzhao of Huxi, number 33060, and Sun Quanzhao's head was crushed. Blood gushed out like a tide. Officer number 79 of the French Concession was present and witnessed the event, recorded the car number, detained the person at the French Concession Police Station, and sent the crushed rickshaw puller to the hospital. He died before he could be rescued. His mother, Sun Chen, because her son died tragically and was destitute, and the orphaned children and widows, etc., had no means of livelihood, had submitted a request to Mayor Wu of the city to forward a letter to the British Consulate in Shanghai for quick compensation, but had not received a reply. Yesterday afternoon at 3 pm, at a certain elementary school on Xieqiao in Nanshi, she invited fellow villagers Feng Guomin, Meng Zhaoxiong, Chen Guobin, Wang Weigao, Xue Zengfu, Feng Shuheng, Chen Zishan, and others to request assistance. Sun Chen reported the circumstances of her son Sun Quanzhao's tragic death. After speaking, tears fell like rain. As a result, the Yangzhou Bayi fellow villagers in Shanghai formed the Sun Quanzhao Victim Support Committee and elected Feng Guomin, Chen Guobin, Wang Weigao, and others to submit a petition to the municipal government, etc., to request the quick forwarding of a letter to the British Consul for negotiation and quick compensation.

Mixed Cargoes, Continued Extension for Half a Year, Approved to Be Implemented from July 1st 127

Previously, in order to meet the needs of merchants along the two railways and facilitate small-scale operations, the Ministry of Railways approved a special relaxation of the restrictions on mixed loading of freight cars to ten types. Since the trial implementation, the term has been extended repeatedly. Now, as it is about to expire at the end of June of this year, there is still a need for an extension in fact. Therefore, the Ministry of Railways instructed with Order No. 5346 of the Industry Department, approving a continued extension for six months from July 1st. However, intermodal cargoes should still be limited to five types according to regulations.

Xu Yi and Others Accused Case, Court Discusses Delivery of 5,000 Yuan Cash Bail 130

Lawyer Xu Yi, residing at No. 17, Lane 71, Tangshan Road, has been practicing law in Shanghai. Recently, together with his younger brother Xu Yiming, his father-in-law Zhao Dong, and Ye Rumei, he was sued by Li Quanshen, manager of the China Gengtai Hehe Flour Mill, and lawyers Li Shirui and Li Lin for stealing seals, fraud, breach of contract, etc. in the First Special Court, with attached civil lawsuits. The reasons for the prosecution stated that the defendant Xu Yi, while practicing law, also served as a staff member of the plaintiff Gengtai Hehe Flour Mill and had established Rongxingkang Coal Company to purchase coal raw materials for the Gengtai Mill. As of January of the 23rd year, Gengtai owed the Coal Company more than 30,000 yuan. He continued to issue Xu Yi 21 checks, which could not be cashed upon maturity. The amount, plus interest, calculated to the end of December, totaled more than 37,000 yuan. Xu then requested Gengtai to replace the November 10th checks with three papers, which were issued by the accounting room Ye Rumei. However, the original 11 papers have not been returned. The Gengtai Mill refused to cash them because it could not pay one paper twice. In January of the 23rd year, Xu Yi, claiming to be the Zhonghe Bank, used the name of the legal representative Zhao Pei to file a lawsuit in the First Special Court, accusing Gengtai manager Li Quanshen of abusing checks and fabricating facts to deceive the court. He won the lawsuit and intensified his efforts to request the seizure of the residences of Cheng Linsheng and Cheng Yize in order to obtain illegal benefits. Fortunately, the court saw through his deceit and did not execute it. The plaintiff Li Quanshen believed that the above-mentioned three papers should not be cashed and should request the court to investigate according to law. On the previous day, magistrate Jiang Shuzi ascended to the criminal court to conduct a joint interrogation. First, the plaintiff stated the above, and only the defendants Xu Yi and Xu Yiming appeared in court. According to the supply, the item check was transferred by Xu Yiming to Zhao Pei. Because it could not be cashed, Zhao filed a lawsuit in court, and the plaintiff's director Xu Yi buried it on behalf of Zhao. He reconciled in court. The court asked Xu Yi whether the lawyer's power of attorney issued by Zhao Pei was written by him. Xu admitted that several were written by him and asked where Zhao Pei was now. Xu Yi replied that his documents were collected by lawyer Wang Jianhang, and Wang was also in court today, please ask him directly. Wang Jianhang was summoned to court and said that Zhao Pei was now in Suzhou. Magistrate Jiang reviewed the situation and believed that the content of the case was complicated and still needed to be testified and the previous case files transferred. He then ordered a rescheduling for further interrogation at 2:00 pm on the 28th of this month. Xu Yi paid 5,000 yuan bail and, before submitting a formal bail bond, was temporarily entrusted to his defense lawyer He Baqian to be responsible for bailing him out, and was limited to submitting a bail bond the next day.

Hengda Factory Invents New Fireboat 132

The Hengda Fire Engine Manufacturing Factory at No. 697 Zhejiang Road in this city is a factory specializing in the manufacture of firefighting equipment founded by Mr. Le Jinlan, a Chinese national. Its Jinlan brand fire pumps of various kinds have been sold for more than 20 years and have a good reputation. The factory, in view of the fact that firefighting tools in various parts of China mainly focus on land use and often delay due to detours, has now invented a new and practical motor fireboat after research. It is 26 feet long, weighs 9,000 pounds, has 60 horsepower, and a speed of 35 miles. It is equipped with a double-leaf gallon oil pump that can discharge water from four angles at the same time. The equipment is very complete, including ladders, alarm bells, fire extinguishers, life jackets, and first aid kits. It is also equipped with a radio to facilitate the transmission of news. It is currently being rushed to production and will be launched this month. It is said that the factory will invite all sectors to visit and then conduct trials in inland areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, which is truly good news for society.

Landlord Assaults Tenant Case Concluded 133

Shi Agen from Yangzhou, residing at No. 11, Lane 320, Meizhou Road, planned to move elsewhere at about 6:00 am on the 8th of this month, but the landlord, Xu Jintao, a local, and his wife and son Hao Liang refused, saying that he had to repay the 10 yuan usury loan he had guaranteed. They quarreled with each other. As a result, he was violently beaten, suffered serious injuries, and fell to the ground crying for help. Hua Pu and detectives of No. 2494 arrived and, when Xu Jintao and his wife took the opportunity to escape, arrested their son and took him to the Yangshupu Police Station for detention. The injured person was sent to Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment. The next morning, he was escorted to the First Special District Court. Because Shi Agen's injury had not yet arrived, Wang Yaotang stated the previous situation and requested an investigation. Subsequently, the victim Shi Agen claimed that the defendant's father had guaranteed only 10 yuan for the loan and should not have beaten him so severely. He still felt abnormal pain in his head and chest and demanded that the defendant be punished. Xu Haoliang claimed that he had beaten his mother first at the time and begged for forgiveness while evading the issue. Magistrate Wu ordered him to be detained again and scheduled a sentence. Shi Agen was sent to the forensic office to examine the injuries.

Dalai Nanhua Firm and Others Petition for the Construction of Luban Road 134

The road conditions of Luban Road in Lujiawan, Nanshi are poor, and dust is flying. More than 70 merchants and residents, including the Meiya Dyeing and Finishing Factory, Guanghua Textile Factory, Dalai Nanhua Firm, and Changle Chinese Pharmacy, have separately submitted petitions to the Public Works Bureau, Health Bureau, and Public Utilities Bureau, urging them to repair the road, sprinkle water, and reduce the speed of public buses. The petition to the Public Works Bureau stated that the merchants and residents have lived on Luban Road for many years, but the decline of the market is all due to the poor road conditions. When it is sunny, dust obscures the eyes; when it rains, mud covers the ankles. Pedestrians regard it as a dangerous road, and commerce cannot develop. We eagerly hope that the Bureau will repair the road, and we are leading without a day. Before the Public Utilities Bureau had repaired the road, it abruptly put public buses into operation on May 1st. For the sake of prospering the market, the transportation aspect can be said to be very beneficial. However, the merchants and residents on both sides are even more burdened by the ravages of dust and sand. Drivers are inconsiderate and only seek speed. Therefore, every car that passes raises dust over the eaves. This goes back and forth, and there is no peace for a moment all day long. Therefore, we urge the Bureau to quickly repair the Luban Road route and request that the Public Utilities Bureau reduce the speed of travel before the road is repaired in order to benefit merchants, travelers, and travelers, and be moved by virtue.

Maid Sent to Relief Association for Care 136

Huang Adong, a woman from Jiaxing, is 15 years old. Her parents died when she was young. At the age of nine, she was sold by her clan uncle to Huang Houliang, the owner of Dechangqin Cloth Shop at No. 9, Tongfang Lane, Fujian Road, as a maid for 70 yuan. It has been six years since then. On the morning of the previous day, Huang suddenly fled and threw himself to the Laozha Patrol House requesting relief. After the patrol was dispatched, Detective Yin Sijiu was ordered to investigate. According to the woman, she had been raped three times by her owner since the winter solstice of last year, and she escaped to seek freedom because she could not bear the suffering. The patrol house, being inconvenient to deal with, sent her to the criminal court of the First Special District Court for disposal yesterday morning. The patrol house's lawyer, Ru Bao Yi, explained the previous situation and said that Huang Adong was only 15 years old and her development was not yet complete, but she suffered such trampling. Unless Huang herself sues, the patrol house will pursue the matter. Qian Hongye, the court president, questioned Huang. According to her, she was treated well since she was sold to Huang Houliang's family. The court questioned whether she had been raped twice and whether she wanted to sue. She replied that she had indeed been raped once, but did not want to sue. She went to the patrol house yesterday with the owner's concubine. President Qian then ordered Huang Adong to be sent to the Relief Association for care.

The contract has not yet been signed, but the deposit has been paid and the takeover has begun.

Municipal Citizens Advocate for National Products Association: New Venue to Hold Opening Ceremony; Rescuing Factories, Promoting National Products, Donating Goods to Establish Schools, and Providing Medical Treatment 141

The Shanghai Municipal Citizens Advocate for National Products Association, since planning and establishing its new venue, has been underway for several months. All the construction work has been designed and executed by Executive Committee Member Mr. Xu Jianruo, and has now been completed. The interior decoration is under active preparation. The opening ceremony will be held on the 15th anniversary of the Association's founding. It is recently learned that the Association's work is progressing rapidly. The following is a record of various news items:

Rescuing Factories

The Association believes that national product factories are in an unfavorable market environment, with goods being difficult to sell and economic turnover severely impacted. Therefore, Executive Committee Member Mr. Chen Yiting was recommended to repeatedly present proposals, visiting Finance Minister Kong, Vice Minister Xu, and leaders in the banking industry, requesting credit loans to be liberally extended to national product factories for rescue. Minister Kong has accepted this proposal and has already issued a notice to the affiliated factories, urging them to fill out the required loan amounts for reporting.

Literacy School

The Association, upon receiving instructions from the Municipal Government, is preparing to establish the Shanghai Private No. 302 Literacy School. Secretary Huang Mengtu has been appointed to be in charge, Clerk Wu Zishi will serve as a teacher, and Clerk Chen Guoming will recruit students. Classes are scheduled to begin on July 1st, from 5:00 PM to 6:00 PM. Executive Committee Member Shao Daren will donate textbooks, desks, and chairs, and Xu Yunhui will donate blackboards and other school supplies. Various Executive Committee members will donate student supplies such as pens, ink, stone tablets, paper, and notebooks, enthusiastically supporting the literacy movement, which is commendable. It is reported that, in addition to teaching according to regulations, the school will schedule national product industry leaders to give two lectures each week, supplementing extracurricular knowledge.

Providing Medical Treatment and Medication

As summer approaches, epidemics are rampant, and the common people are unable to afford medical treatment for infections. In order to protect the health of its members and safeguard the well-being of the common people, the Association has hired traditional Chinese medicine doctors specializing in internal medicine, ENT, gynecology, and pediatrics, such as Yuan Rongqing, to provide regular free consultations at the Association from 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM every afternoon. Medication will be provided free of charge every week, dispensed according to prescriptions by Yu Qing Tang on Avenue Paul Beau. The Association will also collect epidemic prevention and emergency medicines such as Rendan, Shengdan, Ten Drops Water, and Two Days Oil, produced by its member pharmaceutical factories, for daily distribution, benefiting the people and contributing to public health.

Promoting National Products

The Association believes that affiliated factories are affected by the social economy, resulting in sluggish sales and accumulated products. This is of great significance to the national economy and the people's livelihood. After repeated emergency meetings, plans for promotion were decided: (1) Collect exquisite products from various factories, set up a room for display, invite representatives of various trade associations in Shanghai to visit and compare, and encourage procurement; (2) Send letters to chambers of commerce across the country, urging stores to promote national products and make efforts to publicize national products; (3) Telegraph the party and government organs of various provinces, cities, and counties, leading the organization of national product exhibitions and instructing the public to use national products exclusively; (4) Petition the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to fix the tariff committee, increasing import tariffs on foreign goods, reducing all taxes on national products, and implementing rewards for national product production.

It Rained Again Yesterday: Rice Prices Plunge by Eighty Cents; Farmers Had Already Sold Their Harvest, Not Affected; With Another Rain, Rice Prices Will Fall Further 142

Previously, since the beginning of summer, rainfall has been scarce, and seedlings of rice and cotton have mostly died due to drought, threatening a drought disaster. As a result, rice prices in the city continued to rise, reaching a peak of 13.90 yuan. On the 16th of this month, rice-producing areas in various regions rejoiced in timely rain, and rice prices gradually declined. It is estimated that rice prices fell by one cent on the 16th, four cents on the 17th, and two cents on the 18th. Yesterday, according to a reporter from the China News Agency, rice prices fell another one cent, totaling a drop of eighty cents in four days. According to rice boat owners in Nanshi, the continuous drop in rice prices has not affected the rural economy, as most farmers had already sold their stored rice, benefiting the livelihood of the poor. However, yesterday's market prices were highest for Changshu premium japonica rice at 12.70 yuan, and lowest for Yin rice from various regions at around 10.20 yuan. Furthermore, it rained again yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM. The previous rainfall was still insufficient, but yesterday's rain greatly benefited agricultural production, so rice prices are expected to continue to fall.

Previously, a strange man of unknown name and nationality was arrested in this port. The Chinese authorities had repeatedly requested extradition. The authorities of the Public Concession, noting that the suspect had been repeatedly requested for extradition by the Chinese authorities and that there was no evidence of his name or nationality, and that he had been detained for a long time, immediately instructed the police to hand over the suspect to the Chinese authorities for interrogation.

Niu Yongjian and Others Develop Seaside Bathing Beach, Discover Ancient Ming Dynasty Well: Located at Qijiadun, 80 Kilometers from Shanghai; Pure Water Still Full at a Depth of Ten Feet 145

Riri News reports that Qijiadun, Songjiang County, is located more than 80 kilometers from this port and is situated on the coast, making it a natural seawater bathing beach. A large-scale seaside bathing beach was initiated by Central Committee Member Niu Yongjian and more than ten local gentry, including Zhang Mingguang. Construction began last month, and it was planned to dig several wells near the bathing beach. A few days ago, while several workers were digging, they suddenly discovered an ancient well at a depth of more than ten feet, filled with clear water. According to the speculation of a certain historian, it was likely left over from the late Ming Dynasty, as this area was the region where General Qi Jiguang defended against Japanese pirates during the Ming Dynasty. This has caused a sensation in the surrounding areas, and people have been rushing to the site to visit in recent days. It indeed has value for research by general archaeologists.

Shanghai Telephone Bureau's Recent Business Development Plan 146

Due to the increasing number of users and the growing volume of calls, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications needs to develop its engineering business to achieve effective coordination. According to reports:

Increased Relay Lines in Wusong: The bureau considers the Wusong branch to be located north of the city center. The original five pairs of relay lines to the Zhabei branch are gradually becoming insufficient. Currently, two more pairs are being added. For simplicity and economy, it is planned to connect to the city center branch. It is said that from the first of last month, the original Zhabei automatic telephone number 41181 of the branch was changed to the city center number 77181 to facilitate call traffic.

Increased Automatic Switchboard in Longhua: The bureau notes the increasing number of users in the Longhua area. The area is adjacent to the concessions, and there are many factories. The need for telephones is also very urgent. The branch originally had a 150-line automatic switchboard, which has been filled. Therefore, the bureau is planning to add more to facilitate expansion. Once the plan is drafted and approved, procurement and installation can begin.

Planning Multiple-User Line: The bureau plans to modify the existing equipment in the Nanshi and Zhabei bureaus to install multiple-user lines. It is said that this improvement is entirely for the convenience of citizens. For example, three or four households in a residence or farm can share a line, which is economical for both the bureau and users. This method is called a multiple-user line. It is still in the initial stages in China. It is said that it is planned to modify 500 numbers in Nanshi and 200 numbers in Zhabei as a trial. The proposal is currently submitted to the Ministry for approval for implementation.

Publishing New Telephone Directory: The bureau's new telephone directory for this year is about to be printed. It is said that there have been many improvements in this compilation. It is expected to be published around July 1st for distribution to users.

Xin Hua Bank Robbery Case Trial Record: How Did Zhu Boyan's Gun Fall into the Hands of the Thieves? Bullet Shells Recovered by Police Not Presented Yesterday 147

On the morning of the 4th of this month, at around 10:00 AM, the Xiafei Road Fourth Branch of the Shanghai Xin Hua Trust and Savings Bank at No. 500 Avenue Joffre in the French Concession was suddenly stormed by three armed robbers, who stole 4,766.70 yuan in cash. As the robbers fled with the loot, detectives pursued them. They fled into the Hehe Lane, firing their guns to resist arrest, killing Wang Yan, a Yangzhou woman hired by the Wang family at No. 40 of the lane, and wounding Xue Guoxun, a guard at No. 309 of the lane. They then fled into the Public Concession at No. 67 Chongqing Road, where an unnamed male construction worker was killed by a stray bullet. As a result, the robbers fled into the Ma'an Lane at No. 188 Chongqing Road. The robber Wang Zhiting (also known as Wang Diting, aged 20), a young man from Anhui, was arrested in the kitchen of the Bao family at No. 27 of the lane. A gun and five bullets were found in the woodpile. He was taken to the Chengdu Road Police Station. Detectives from the French police station brought Wang back to the court for interrogation and investigation. The French police later found the gun's serial number. The gun belonged to Zhu Boyan, a native of Haiyan, Zhejiang, who resided at No. 31 Continental Terrace on Rue Albert. It was suspected that Zhu had supplied the thieves with firearms. He was arrested and sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation. He was ordered to pay a 3,000 yuan bail and report when summoned for joint investigation and handling. The case had been reported in this newspaper. The police investigation has now been completed. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, Judge Sun Pengxian of the Second Special District Court, accompanied by Clerk Tao Zongkan, came to the Criminal Court to conduct the trial. The ten robbers and Zhu were ordered to be brought to the case. First, Yao Zhaodi, the lawyer of the Police Department, stated the case, briefly stating that, according to the police investigation, the first defendant, Wang Zhiting, and his accomplices Zhang Zifa and Chen Zilin, jointly committed the robbery. Wang threatened the bank employees with a gun, Zhang robbed the money, and Chen acted as a lookout at the entrance. After the robbery, they fled with the loot, firing their guns to resist arrest and killing people. Wang was arrested, and the gun was seized. It has been verified that no bullet shells were found, and this gun is not the same. Therefore, the shooting and killing of people are not related to the defendant Wang Zhiting in this case. He is now being prosecuted under Article 348 of the Criminal Law for armed robbery by a group of three people. As for the second defendant, Zhu Boyan, the gun seized was found to be his property. According to Zhu, he gave the gun to a Jin surname friend introduced by a Qiu surname friend from Shanqiu last year. However, the gun was not licensed. He is now being prosecuted under Article 164 of the Criminal Law for disrupting public order and Article 2 of the Regulations for the Suppression of Military and Civilian Firearms. The court is requested to interrogate and investigate. The judge then interrogated Wang, who claimed that he came to Shanghai in December last year and met Zhang Zifa at the Xujiahui Weaving Factory. In February this year, he lost his job. He was working at the Sixteen Pups Wharf when Zhang came to call him to chat at the Panjia Wood Bridge Tea House. Later, they went to Avenue Joffre and met Chen. Zhang pushed me in. I didn't dare to jump. I don't know if Chen had a gun. I didn't switch the gun I was holding, and I didn't fire it. At this point, the court summoned the plaintiff Chen Bugao (the director of the Xin Hua branch, a native of Guangdong) to the front of the court to inquire about the robbery. Chen said that when the robbers came in to rob, I was on the phone. The robber stepped forward, snatched the phone from my hand, and threatened me with a gun. Then I saw the robber jump into the counter and search for banknotes. A tall robber was standing at the door. All three robbers were wearing long coats and holding guns. The robber in the case seemed to be the one who jumped into the counter. The judge then summoned Detective Zhou Buguang, who was responsible for handling the case, to describe the arrest of the defendant. Zhou said that Wang escaped from the roof of the kitchen at No. 27, Lane 88, Chongqing Road. Zhang Chen, a tenant in the house, was lying in bed after giving birth. She heard the sound of lead sheets on the roof and called the tenant Shou Qing to go outside to look. Bao then reported to the detectives, who arrested Wang. The judge ordered the bailiffs to take Zhu Boyan to the waiting room behind the court. He separately interrogated the main offender and asked if he knew Zhu and knew where Zhang Zifa's gun came from. Wang said that he did not know Zhu and did not know the source of Zhang's gun. The judge then ordered Zhu Boyan to be brought to the case. Zhu claimed that he was the secretary of the Ming Hua Bank. Although the bank is currently closed for liquidation, he has not left his position. The gun was indeed my property. The gun was given to me by Shi Jinsheng, a friend from the Gold Exchange, seven or eight years ago. Because I was working at the bank, I had a gun for self-defense. Later, a friend gave me a six-inch pistol, which was more beautiful than this gun. I applied for a license from the Public Security Bureau of the Chinese Concession and the British and French Concessions. This gun was kept at home and not used, so I did not get a license. In April last year, a neighbor had Communist hideouts. The French police came to search and found the gun in my house. After investigation, it was proved that I was a legitimate businessman and the gun was returned. Later, Qiu Zipei, the owner of the Xinchang Customs Brokerage on Shandong Road and Jinjiang Street, who was a friend for ten years, introduced me to a friend, Jin Cixiang. This person used to serve as a division commander under He Chengjun, the chairman of Hubei Province. He was doing business in Shanghai. I have known him for three years. Because it was inconvenient to keep the gun at home, I gave the gun to Jin Cixiang. I asked, "Do you know where Jin lives?" He replied, "He used to write me a note with an address: Dachen Gold Shop, Dean Lane, Yipentang Lane." I have never been there and don't know how the gun fell into the hands of the bandits. He also hired a lawyer to defend him in court. At this point, because the police had not submitted the bullet shells found at the scene of the shooting for inspection, the court ordered a postponement until the 28th of this month for further interrogation. The defendant Wang Zhiting was returned to custody. Zhu Boyan remained under the original bail, and Detective Zhou Buguang of the police station was informed to submit the bullet shells found at the next hearing for inspection. The court adjourned.

Police Suppress Disguised Gambling Devices; Kwong Sang Hong Sued for Disobeying the Law 148

In order to cater to the gambling psychology of the general public, businesses such as dance halls, restaurants, and barber shops in this city have installed a novel device resembling a square box with holes on the top and bottom. When someone plays with it, they put a two-cent coin into the top hole and turn the crank. If the coin falls into the winning slot, a token in the shape of a coin will suddenly drop out of the bottom hole. Players can exchange the token for cash. Because this device is not made in China, it does not have a Chinese name. Someone has coined the name "Dui Hua Ji" for it. As the machine becomes popular, it spreads quickly and is adopted by more and more people. Seeing its harm is great, the public security authorities of the public concession, realizing that it is a disguised gambling device, have ordered all police stations to strictly prohibit it in their respective jurisdictions. If found, they will be ordered to dismantle it. Therefore, there are few installers at present, and it is not difficult to eliminate it completely. However, the Kwong Sang Hong branch at No. 156 Henan Road still disregards the ban. Not only does it not dismantle the machine, but it also installs it in a very conspicuous place in the store, attracting customers to enthusiastically gamble. The responsible detectives Su Changsheng and Li Yijian of the police station found that the store owner, Xi Guangsheng, was gambling for profit, violating Article 280 of the Criminal Law and Article 45 of the Municipal Council's police regulations. They reported it to the First Special District Local Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Huang Risheng summoned him for trial. The defendant, Xi Guangsheng, refused to appear in court and sent an employee, Tang Miao, to appear. He claimed that Xi had gone to another port and requested a postponement. However, according to the reports of detectives Su and Li, Xi was indeed in Shanghai. Zhang Shuaizhu, the police lawyer, made a statement. The court ordered a postponement of seven days for further interrogation. If Xi Guangsheng still fails to appear in court by the deadline, he will be arrested according to the law.

Preventing Suicide: Director of Social Affairs Continues to Express Opinions; Serious Unemployment Problem Difficult to Solve; Assistance to Be Provided to Those in Need 150

Mr. Wu Xingya, director of the Social Affairs Bureau of this city, previously expressed his views on preventing suicide. Since it was published in this newspaper, it has attracted deep attention from all parties. Numerous letters have been sent to Mr. Wu, requesting assistance to avoid suicide. In addition to sending personnel to investigate for disposition, Mr. Wu has supplemented his previous remarks with the following views, which are recorded by a reporter from Shenshi News: Since the various newspapers disclosed my opinion on preventing suicide on the 9th of this month, I have been deeply impressed by the sympathy of public opinion and the generosity of those who have offered advice. For example, the editorial of the Xinwen News advocates cultivating the national perseverance and fundamentally eliminating the thought of suicide in peacetime. The commentary in Shenbao promotes restraining self-centeredness, fostering a national concept, and the highest ideal of benefiting the people, to save the decadent trend of suicide, extending my theory of psychological transformation, with profound implications, are all immutable arguments. As for the section on practical assistance, there are still few insightful views from all parties for reference. Indeed, in the autumn of public and private economic difficulties, the number of people in urgent need of rescue is limitless. Mentioning practical assistance gives the feeling of "How can I get tens of millions of rooms to shelter all the poor scholars in the world!" For example, in this week alone, more than twenty letters have been sent to me, detailing their suffering and requesting assistance, otherwise they will commit suicide. Among them, in addition to a small number due to debts ranging from dozens to hundreds of yuan, requesting to pay on their behalf, the vast majority are due to prolonged unemployment, unable to make a living, requesting to be introduced to a job. At this time, mentioning the issue of unemployment is a truly extremely serious and extremely complex social problem. Suppose the Social Affairs Bureau, to the best of its ability, first registers the unemployed and then introduces them to jobs. If it is to be effective, then all industrial and commercial sectors, all employment agencies, must be willing to cooperate with the Social Affairs Bureau and employ its registered people as much as possible, which is one thing. The market is turning prosperous, and various industries do need to add personnel, which is another thing. The people needed by various industries and the people registered by the Social Affairs Bureau must have compatible conditions, which is another thing. The unemployed themselves must not have major defects in terms of physical strength, knowledge, and morality, which is another thing. Therefore, the problems involved in the unemployment issue are so extensive that they cannot be solved by the efforts of one Social Affairs Bureau. Even the authorities in Europe and the United States today are racking their brains and cannot solve it. As for those who suffer from economic oppression, live in poverty, and are not due to their own faults, I am willing to provide assistance to those who have been verified. However, in the current situation, the first thing to do is nothing more than the following points: One is to provide them with funds to send themselves or their entire family back to their place of origin, so as to avoid wandering outside. One is to lend them funds through the Lending Office to enable them to make a living on their own. One is to send their children to childcare institutions for education, to reduce their burden. In short, at a time when the country is in trouble and the people are poor, we can only rely on the general public to have a share of heart, do a share of heart, have a share of strength, and do a share of strength, to prevent suicide and reverse the tragedy. Those who have suffered misfortune should also fundamentally change their minds, strengthen themselves, work hard and strive to overcome the difficulties.

Road Police Seize Smuggled Drugs; Bonus Distribution Method Promulgated by the Ministry of Railways 152

In order to reward railway police agencies for seizing smuggled opium and narcotics, the Ministry of Railways yesterday issued a special order promulgating measures for the distribution of rewards. 1. For all railway police agencies that seize smuggled opium and narcotics, the distribution of bonuses allocated by local anti-smoking agencies or fines imposed by court judgments should be handled in accordance with the following provisions: 2. In order to prepare for police public welfare undertakings and to reward police officers who have made exceptional efforts in cracking down on smoking cases, or to subsidize the purchase of cable lines, public reserve funds should be appropriately drawn from this bonus fund and stored for future use. The amount of public reserve and the percentage of awards shall be in accordance with the following provisions: (1) Less than 50 yuan, no public reserve is required; 50 yuan or more but less than 100 yuan, 12% is set aside as public reserve, and 80% is distributed as awards; (2) 100 yuan or more but less than 200 yuan, 25% is set aside as public reserve, and 75% is distributed as awards; (3) 200 yuan or more but less than 400 yuan, 30% is set aside as public reserve, and 70% is distributed as awards; (4) 400 yuan or more but less than 600 yuan, 35% is set aside as public reserve, and 65% is distributed as awards; (5) 600 yuan or more, 40% is set aside as public reserve, and 60% is distributed as awards. 3. All public reserve funds shall be managed by a management committee organized by the police department. 4. The bonus for those who seized and handled the case, in addition to deducting the public reserve, the percentage of awards is as follows: (1) Those who first reported and thus seized the case shall receive 20%; (2) The police officer who personally seized the case shall receive 35%; (3) The personnel who handled the seizure at the segment/team level shall receive a total of 20%; (4) The personnel who handled the seizure at the police section/road protection brigade level shall receive a total of 15%; (5) The personnel who handled the seizure at the police department/office level shall receive a total of 10%. 5. Anyone who personally seized the case without relying on reports from others shall be entitled to both items 1 and 2 of the preceding article. Where there is no police section/road protection brigade, the bonus under item 4 shall be transferred to the public reserve fund. 6. If the number of persons involved in items 1 to 5 listed in Article 4 is two or more, the bonus received should be divided equally. 7. If the seizure is made jointly with personnel from other departments, in addition to drawing the public reserve fund, half of the remaining bonus should be transferred to the agency that jointly seized the case, and the remaining half should be handled in accordance with Article 4. (8). If personnel from other departments seize and transfer the case to the police agencies of various roads for handling, all bonuses, in addition to drawing the public fund, shall be transferred to the personnel of other departments in accordance with items 1 and 2 of Article 4, and the remainder shall be handled in accordance with Article 4. 8. If the perpetrators of smoking cases are sent to the court, but are not fined, or are unable to pay the fine even if fined, and are legally converted to imprisonment or labor service, all police officers who have contributed to the case may be appropriately rewarded by the police station from the public reserve fund, and reported to the Road Police Management Office for approval, and then notified to the Public Reserve Fund Management Committee for allocation. 10. After the promulgation of these measures, all temporary measures previously formulated by the road bureaus of various roads shall be abolished. 11. These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation of the Ministry's order.

Famous Painter Li Xia Holds Solo Exhibition 159

Li Xia of Xianyou is a great artist of the contemporary era. He is capable of painting everything, and his figure painting is particularly profound. He has dabbled in the doors and courtyards of Piaozi, Xinluo, Shangguan Zhou, and other families, and after glimpsing his hall, he suddenly gained something, and then he left in a fluttering manner, not constrained by it. Last year, Chairman Xiong of Jiangxi was going to paint 100 portraits of famous sages. Hearing of Mr. Li's name, he happily invited him. At first, he did not want to go, but the chairman asked Mr. Li's fellow villagers to convey his earnest invitation, so he set off. When he arrived in Ganzhou, he was warmly welcomed. Mr. Li was uninhibited and repeatedly resigned, but the chairman insisted on keeping him. After more than half a year, he resolutely returned east and responded to the ten requests of his countrymen in the capital to exhibit copies of his portraits of famous sages. In a few days, they were all sold out. Chairman Lin of the National Government deeply appreciated it and collected many of them exclusively. After the exhibition, he returned to Shanghai. The collection office accumulated several cases of paper and silk, and he wielded his brush day and night, month after month. Whenever he was in the mood, he kept one or two pictures for his own enjoyment. After a long time, he accumulated dozens or hundreds of pictures. Mr. Li's friends and celebrities from all over the sea strongly encouraged him to hold an exhibition at the Sanshan Hall on Fourth Avenue starting today (the 20th) to share with his fellow enthusiasts, lasting until the 24th. It is expected that poets and painters from all over the sea will follow in droves.
