Free Talk

Reading "A Textual Research on the Deeds of Yang Yao" 172

— Cao Juren

"The Deeds of Yang Yao" was written by Song Dingfeng, a recluse, and is found in Yue Ke's "Jintuo Zucbian." Mr. Zhu Xizu's annotated and researched edition was recently published by the Commercial Press. In his preface, Mr. Zhu Xizu says: "During the reign of Emperor Gaozong of the Southern Song Dynasty, there were events similar to the present situation. For example, the area north of the Yellow River was lost to the Jin invaders. The Jin also established Liu Yu as the puppet emperor of the Qi dynasty in Shandong, Henan, and Shaanxi, with the reign title 'Fuyuan,' which is one similarity. The Song Dynasty, between the Huai and Han Rivers and the Yangtze River, imitated the Tang Dynasty's frontier military governors by setting up more than ten pacification commissioners as a barrier, but they were divided and occupied territory, dividing military strength. Some did not obey orders, attacked and annexed each other, or surrendered to the puppet Qi, borrowing external forces for internal invasion, which is another similarity. Moreover, Zhong Xiang and Yang Yao advocated the doctrine of equalizing wealth and poverty, gathering a crowd of 400,000, spreading across land and water for thousands of miles, which is a third similarity. All of these can serve as a mirror for today." Mr. Zhu Xizu is a thoughtful person. Besides the textual research on the deeds of Yang Yao, he also wants to write a "Veritable Records of the Puppet Qi Dynasty" and a "Study on the Pacification Commissioners of the Early Southern Song Dynasty," hoping to gain insight into the underlying chaos of the time. We believe this is very meaningful.

Zhong Xiang and Yang Yao advocated "equalizing wealth and poverty and equalizing the noble and the base." "Equalizing wealth and poverty" was originally a Confucian idea. Confucius said, "Do not worry about scarcity, but worry about inequality." Whenever the issue of land distribution is mentioned, no one since Dong Zhongshu and Liu Xin has not dreamed of realizing the well-field system. Even in the early Ming Dynasty, Fang Xiaoru advocated restoring the well-field system, which was used by Prince Yan Di as a slogan to attack Emperor Jianwen. Since the successful implementation of the equal-field system in the Northern Wei Dynasty, discussions about land reform have generally followed this path. The idea of equalizing wealth and poverty is deeply imprinted in everyone's mind. Therefore, those who rose up in the mountains and among the people always carried a touch of "equalizing wealth and poverty," intentionally or unintentionally. For example, Li Zicheng, the roving bandit of the late Ming Dynasty, was universally regarded as a ruthless villain, but his proclamation to attack the Ming Dynasty stated:

"...Now, your Ming Dynasty has long occupied its position, and the laws and regulations have been relaxed. The ruler is not very wise, isolated and often surrounded by deceit. The officials are all self-serving, colluding in factions, and there is very little public loyalty. Bribes run rampant in the government, and the power and blessings of the court are shifting daily. The gentry monopolize profits, and the people's resources are almost exhausted. Heaven has exhausted its love for the people, causing fleeing people to suffer from disasters. I rose from the common people, witnessing the haggard faces and feeling the pain myself. Considering that all the people in the land are suffering from poverty, how can I bear to easily abandon the mountains and rivers, and not relieve them from the fire and water?...”

This proclamation confused many scholar-officials in Beijing at the time, and everyone wrote articles to refute the rumors, saying: "...(The bandit leader) steals the false reputation of benevolence and righteousness and spreads the reality of violence." Zhong Xiang and Yang Yao implemented the equalization of wealth and poverty more purposefully and effectively. They "burned government offices, cities, temples, and the homes of the wealthy, killing officials, Confucian scholars, monks, Taoists, doctors, and shamans." (Mr. Zhu Xizu said: "Burning government offices and killing officials was to eliminate evil laws; burning cities was to eliminate wealthy merchants; burning the homes of the wealthy was to eliminate annexation; killing Confucian scholars was to eliminate arguments about evil laws; burning temples and killing Taoists, shamans, and other idle people was to eliminate religion and those who do not work; only farmers and workers were not killed because they all support themselves by their own labor." This is a very good explanation.) This was more effective in winning people's hearts than Li Zicheng's distribution of the royal treasury to the starving people. They gathered a crowd of 400,000, roaming over a thousand miles. In the early years of the Southern Song Dynasty, the court spent great effort, with famous generals like Yue Fei taking action, and it took more than ten years to quell the rebellion. This was not accidental. The implementation of the equal-field system in the Northern Wei Dynasty and the equalization of wealth and poverty by Yang Yao can be considered the only two practical implementers of the well-field system advocated by Confucianism since ancient times, whether successful or unsuccessful, they are both excellent lessons for studying Chinese social problems.

"The theory of equalizing the noble and the base" also has its origins. Xu Xing of the agricultural school advocated that Yao and Shun should plow and eat with the people. Hui Shi had the idea of abolishing the esteemed. Liezi said that Zichan's older brother Gongsun Chao loved wine, and his younger brother Gongsun Mu loved women, which were even greater than Zichan's governance of the country, all implying the equalization of the noble and the base. Bao Sheng of the Western Jin Dynasty advocated "abolishing the ruler," saying: "Ever since the distinction between noble and base was established, people have created sharp tools, causing endless harm of invasion and cutting. People fear that crossbows are not strong enough, armor is not firm enough, spears are not sharp enough, and shields are not thick enough." He also said: "The ruler worries in shackles, and the people suffer in hardship, precisely because the ruler and ministers are established, and hidden evils grow day by day." "Without ruler and without ministers, there would be no competition or management." He believed that if the ruler was abolished, the noble and the base were removed, then even the likes of Jie and Zhou would be ordinary people, and even if their nature was fierce and extravagant, how could they exercise it?" Zhong Xiang believed that laws that distinguish between noble and base were not good laws, which is what Bao Sheng meant. However, equalizing the noble and the base seems easy, but it is even more difficult to implement than equalizing wealth and poverty. Even Zhong Xiang and Yang Yao, who advocated equalizing the noble and the base, could not help but call themselves Great Sage Heavenly Kings, which is also a great contradiction. Some time ago, I saw Yosuke Tsurumi advocate the naturalization of leadership, saying: "The leadership that we can accept in this era is not the kind of person who leads and governs all things on earth alone. It is clear that there are leaders in hundreds of aspects for specific purposes. In this sense, every modern person has the potential, according to their talents, to be a leader for others... When human civilization reaches its peak, it is extremely natural that all humans become leaders and are led." In that case, the so-called "equalizing the noble and the base" has gained a new interpretation.

The above can only be said to be my thoughts after reading. I would like to write another specialized article on the research aspects.

"Madman" and I 173

— Ding

The way people greet my friend A Jin with a kind of malice, calling him "madman," often stirs up a violent indignation in my heart. I feel that they are not only insulting A Jin's personality and harming his life, but also, I believe that insulting and harming him is equivalent to insulting and harming his friends. I am one of A Jin's friends. Therefore, I feel the same pain as A Jin for this matter. My brain is about to explode with anger at the way they bully him, abuse him, mock him, and often treat him with such immoral behavior. From this fact, I deeply understand the direction of their inner lives and the source of human misery. I am convinced that this is one of the characteristics of their inherent defects. Whenever I am touched by this matter, I don't know how to depict the outline of life.

A Jin is a person with an unusually straightforward and unyielding personality. He has always worked in the local court. After working hard for most of his life, he is still just a basic messenger. He is almost fifty years old, but his body is still very strong. He not only has the courage to be a person, but also has the talent to be a person. He not only dares to speak, but also dares to resist. Here, he often quarrels with his colleagues for the sake of others. Although he has been here for many years, he has never asked others for a penny of "extra" benefit. If he discovers anything unfair in front of him, such as cheating people, oppressing people, or threatening people, he will roar at you. If he believes that it is necessary to help others, then no matter how difficult it is, he must help them. In short, among them, he is obviously a peculiar person. He has a certain purpose in living here, and he is not afraid to fight with the environment. Therefore, he is very annoying here. They hate him very much because he hinders their various dirty deeds. Therefore, they regard him as a thorn in their side. Must they pull out this "thorn"? Sure enough, he was finally pulled out by them. But he is not afraid, he still has to live on, to do his work, to speak his words. He shouted and yelled everywhere, arguing with people. As a result, he was still hated by them. People looked at him with contempt, and called him "madman" with malice. This matter makes me feel its own nothingness and cruelty, inhuman, full of the smell of wild love from a century ago. I feel very sorry for my friend. And my conscience teaches me that I cannot remain silent about this matter, it is driving me. And my reason is also directing me, so that I cannot but be active in this matter of a lifelong disaster! For my suffering friend, for our unfortunate fate. Therefore, I stood up to speak out against the injustice for my friend, and also to protest for our survival. I explained to people and defended A Jin. I wanted to use my enthusiasm and that undeniable reason to protest to them, so that they would understand that my friend is not the kind of person they call "madman." And I wanted to fiercely spear them, exposing their dark spots. However, my efforts did not have much effect. Not only did they not listen, but they also thought that I was a madman like A Jin. They said: "How can a good person associate with a madman?" So they concluded that I was a madman. As for me, I don't mind being with the "madman" A Jin. And I will fight and sacrifice for him when necessary. So they were even more afraid and disgusted with me. First, they ostracized me from their social life. Then they used various means to frame me, so that I fell into the same situation as A Jin is currently in. In the beginning, I seemed to feel a little pain and sadness in my heart. The reason is that my job was lost because of this, my rice bowl was broken by others, and my "ordinary" friends were also scared of me, they dared not approach me, fearing that my bad reputation would stain their innocence. So they gradually left me and finally broke off all friendly relations with me. This made me very embarrassed at the time. I once said to them angrily: "Why are your brains so stupid? Why are your guts so cowardly? Why are your eyes so short-sighted?" But there was no result. They would not wake up either. Later, I felt that it was useless to have such friends, we do not need such friends. So my heart was also relieved. From then on, I was determined to live the life that I thought I should live. I always maintained that kind of passionate attitude towards pure friendship. And our exchanges became even closer because of this. I often comforted him and helped him within the possible range so that he would not be annoyed by the poor life. And sometimes I explained to him "where" we were encountering. He was very frank and happy, and he shed tears of gratitude for my sincere friendship. This surprised me very much. Because I know that A Jin is a person who only bleeds and does not cry. How could he cry now? Once, when we were sitting face to face talking about various things, especially when I talked about the tragic stories of the world, sure enough, he couldn't bear it. Those precious tears of the old man, those blood-like tears of the old man, quietly fell on the gloomy, dark, and dirty ground. At that time, I felt a kind of unspeakable joy. Because our lives are even more vigorous because of this. I feel that this unbreakable unity of spirit and emotion, besides arousing our enthusiasm for resistance, we feel nothing about their maliciously ridiculing and insulting us.

Bubble 174

Thoughts of Being a Father 175

— Xun Jiu

Coming home, seeing my own children, constantly clinging to my side, crying and making noise, I can't help but think of my own childhood more than ten years ago. Although this cannot serve as a model for my current education of my children, the stern attitude of my father at the time, under the moral authority controlled by purely feudal ideas, is still firmly engraved in my heart, giving rise to a kind of solemn awe.

I entered primary school at the age of six and graduated at the age of eleven. It can be said that I lived a life of cold bench under the strict control of my father. At that time, the only thing that had the deepest relationship with me and helped my father complete his educational responsibility was a ruler that was always placed next to his desk!

Every day when I came home from primary school, when my father called me with his pure voice, the first thing I saw when I stepped into the study that made my heart tremble was that heavy and clumsy ruler! At this time, I didn't dare to be wild at all. I walked tremblingly to the desk where I sat. Then, those "Three Character Classic," "Hundred Family Surnames," "Analects of Confucius," "Mencius," and many other books besides those from school, were opened one by one and taught me to read slowly. After reading them fluently, I would memorize them. If I encountered difficult or unfamiliar places while memorizing, the ruler would immediately hit my body. I endured the pain and wiped away my tears with my sleeves, but I still mumbled and read until I could read them fluently. I was never spared the hope. In addition to reading, I also spent a lonely life alone under a docile and fearful mentality in terms of playing and eating. Even if I ran into another world by chance, but when I met those companions who were as naughty as little sparrows in the fields, if I wasn't ridden as a horse, then my hat would be snatched away and kicked as a ball. This was the beginning of my blushing and feeling the sadness of being trampled on.

But when I got home, thinking of my unfinished homework, my father's terrible face, and that heavy and clumsy ruler, I couldn't help but reappear in front of my eyes.

The scene of my childhood more than ten years ago is still so clearly and closely in my memory, but seeing the children now, their lively playfulness, and the fact that they don't take reading seriously at all, I can't help but feel a little emotional about my own childhood.

Discussion on "Rebirth of Humorous Literature" 176

— Zhao Xiang

I don't like to read any articles that are soft. What I love are those articles that describe reality. Correct and powerful inspiration for life must be obtained in such works. However, in a depressed environment under the limitation of objective conditions, it is inevitably subject to its relative decisions, and the emergence of humorous literature also has its social factors.

Regarding humorous literature, I have never advocated special promotion, although humorous literature has the function of revealing the ugliness of reality from the side. Because humor is often misused to the point of being unrecognizable. Mr. Hu Feng has a passage on the view of humor:

"First, if we leave "social concern," whether it is silly laughter, cold laughter, or knowing smiles, it will shift people's attention and become some kind of psychological or physiological pleasure. "Laughing for the sake of laughing" will be regarded by the Saturday School as a promising younger brother. Second, even if it is genuine humor, the territory is very small. People in places where bullets are whistling have no time for humor, people who are displaced in the thousands of miles of red land have no time for humor, and unemployed people walking in the streets and alleys have no time for humor...

I think most people agree with Mr. Hu's views. Humor is a kind of helpless compromise. As a way of writing that has to be done, it is possible." As an author, he grasps a subject matter, and he naturally has many ways to express it. When he has to write a little humorously here, he will never be unwise and directly confront reality. Therefore, in-depth satire, highlighting techniques, and changes in forms become the fashion of the time.

Humor and satire do not have any conflict. On the contrary, humor contains satire, and it does not matter if satire contains a little humor.

I do not object to the existence of humor, but I think it is unnecessary to raise the banner of "humorous literature" to promote it. That is, as Mr. Hu Feng said, even if it is genuine humor, the territory is very small.

University Days (7) 177

— By German Storm, Translated by Chen Yinzhi

Something annoying—I don't deny it—is that since I learned to dance, the French tailor has been particularly flattering to me. Whenever he saw me on the street or while walking, he would stop and talk to me loudly for a long time. During the first conversation, he even told me that his grandfather had been the chief stoker in the court of Louis XVI.

"Yes, Mr. Philip," he sighed, while offering me his porcelain snuffbox, "look at how a world declines—but my Nari,—you understand me, Mr. Philip!" He took out a colored checkered handkerchief from his pocket and wiped his little eyes. "There's nothing to be done! I'm a poor man, but that child,—she's my treasure, my sweetheart!" As he spoke, he winked and looked at me with a paternal gaze, as if he wanted to pull me into this declining world too.

Soon, the last dance lesson arrived, and we turned this lesson into a small dance party. Parents were invited to visit our dancing; on my parents' side, only my mother agreed to visit, and my father, as a professional doctor and public doctor of the city, always declined all social invitations. As soon as it got dark, I couldn't wait any longer, and I walked into the hall before the scheduled time; all the candles on the wall lamps and hanging lamps were lit tonight. I closed the door and turned around, only to see Nari standing alone in front of the window with her back to me. The sound of the door closing startled her, and she seemed to be hurriedly taking off a golden ornament from her wrist. When I walked closer to her, I saw that it was a bracelet, and the button was already fastened, but she couldn't open it no matter how hard she tried.

"Just wear it there, Nari!" I said.

"This isn't mine," she replied a little flustered, "Jenny left it here and forgot to take it back."

The bracelet made of dimly lustrous Venetian gold with exquisite rose flowers shone slightly on that dark, thin wrist.

"Since you've put it on, just leave it on!" I said softly.

Nari shook her head sadly, her fingers touching the button again.

"Come on!" I said, "This won't do; let me help you!" I felt her little wrist resting lightly in my hand. I hesitated for a while, my eyes dizzy.

"Please hurry up!" she asked me. The little girl lowered her eyes and stood in front of me, her face flushed.

The button was finally unbuttoned. Nari silently placed the gold bracelet on the windowsill between the flowerpots.

Soon the hall was full of people. Mrs. Bolica also did not give up this opportunity, at least she participated in her daughter's celebration in the capacity of a servant. She wore a newly starched hat, sometimes carrying a basket of pastries, sometimes holding a tea tray, walking among the guests. Finally, the musicians began to play; today there were four musicians sitting at a table. The old dance master beat the tambourine, and Nari took my hand and danced the mazurka. —Look, how we dance! And how comfortably she is in my arms, carelessly stepping her little feet on the floor! I also danced with her, as if the rhythm of the music was pushing me. I seemed to have a painful feeling because today was our last time, and perhaps there would never be another chance to dance together.

Page 13

Sports News

Implementation of Compulsory Education: Detailed Rules for the Outline of Temporary Measures (Continued from Yesterday) 178

Chapter Five: School Buildings and Equipment

Article 19: Newly established short-term primary schools in each elementary school district may fully utilize existing local government offices, ancestral halls, and other buildings. They may also borrow or use private houses. If there are no usable or rentable options, they may temporarily construct extremely simple sheds for use.

Article 20: Each school district should, within ten years, select a suitable location and prepare to build formal school buildings for regular primary schools. Those unable to raise construction funds on their own may receive assistance from the county or municipal government.

Article 21: The equipment of short-term primary schools shall be handled with reference to the equipment of ordinary primary schools. However, desks, chairs, and other items may be of a lower standard than those of primary schools.

Article 22: Each school district should raise sufficient equipment funding within ten years to prepare for the conversion of short-term primary schools into ordinary primary schools with all necessary equipment.

Chapter Six: Funding

Article 23: Compulsory education funding, in urban areas, shall be统筹 (coordinated) by the government. In counties and cities within provincial areas, the principle shall be that the province and county share the burden proportionately. The central government may also provide subsidies based on the circumstances of the provinces and cities. The central government may provide special subsidies for compulsory education funding in remote and impoverished provinces.

Article 24: Provincial and municipal compulsory education funding should be allocated according to local conditions, either from provincial and municipal education funding items, or from a certain percentage of total provincial and municipal revenue, or by designating special funds.

Article 25: County and city compulsory education funding should be allocated according to local conditions, either by designating school properties or special tax revenues, and by encouraging people to donate to the best of their ability.

Chapter Seven: Organizations

Article 26: The implementation of compulsory education shall be managed by the Ministry of Education at the central level, by the competent education administrative organs of provinces and cities at the provincial and municipal levels, and by the departments and bureaus in charge of education administration at the county and city levels.

Article 27: All levels of organizations responsible for compulsory education shall establish compulsory education committees to assist in the implementation of compulsory education. The Ministry of Education shall establish a National Compulsory Education Committee, and its regulations shall be determined by ministerial order. Each province and city shall establish a Provincial/Municipal Compulsory Education Committee, with the head of the provincial/municipal education administrative organ as the chairman, and several respected figures from the education sector shall be appointed as members by the provincial/municipal government. Its organizational rules shall be determined by the provincial/municipal education administrative organ and reported to the Ministry of Education for record. Each county and city shall establish a County/City Compulsory Education Committee, and its organizational rules shall be determined by the provincial education department and approved by the provincial government.

Article 28: The main tasks of compulsory education committees at all levels are as follows:

1. National Compulsory Education Committee: A. Propose and review plans for promoting compulsory education; B. Review all regulations and measures related to compulsory education; C. Assess the performance of provinces and cities in implementing compulsory education.

2. Provincial/Municipal Compulsory Education Committee: A. Formulate provincial/municipal plans for promoting compulsory education; B. Supervise the custody and use of provincial/municipal compulsory education funds and central government subsidies for compulsory education in the province/municipality; C. Formulate annual plans for training teachers; D. Assess the performance of counties and cities in implementing compulsory education.

3. City/County Compulsory Education Committee: A. Formulate city/county plans for promoting compulsory education; B. Supervise the custody and use of city/county compulsory education funds and subsidies from higher-level governments for compulsory education in the county/city; C. Review the budgets and final accounts of compulsory education funds under its jurisdiction; D. Assess the performance of subordinate units in implementing compulsory education.

Article 29: Regarding compulsory education affairs in each elementary school district of cities and counties, the county/city education administrative organ shall appoint one school supervisor for every five to ten elementary school districts to manage it. Their tasks are as follows: 1. Publicize the importance of compulsory education work; 2. Formulate implementation plans for compulsory education in the school district; 3. Raise funds; 4. Prepare budgets; 5. Investigate school-age children; 6. Establish schools; 7. Compel school-age children to enroll; 8. Supervise the improvement of private schools. When the county/city education administrative organ deems it necessary, it may appoint instructors or assistants to guide or assist the school supervisors in handling affairs.

Chapter Eight: Rewards and Penalties

Article 30: The status of compulsory education implementation shall be regarded as a special consideration when evaluating the performance of local administrative personnel.

Article 31: People who donate funds to support compulsory education may be rewarded preferentially in accordance with the reward measures for donating to education.

Article 32: The Ministry of Education shall separately formulate measures for handling rewards and penalties related to the promotion of compulsory education.

Chapter Nine: Supplementary Provisions

Article 33: These detailed rules shall be promulgated by the Ministry of Education and submitted to the Executive Yuan for record and implementation.

Article 34: After the promulgation of these detailed rules, the Outline of Measures for Implementing Nurturing Education in the First Phase and the Outline of Measures for Implementing Short-Term Compulsory Education previously promulgated by the Ministry of Education shall be repealed. (End)

Teachers Strike in the First District of Pinghu 181

In the first district of Pinghu County, which is the urban area, including both inside and outside the city and the Zhou圩 in the northeast, and the General Riding Pond in the southwest, the jurisdiction is vast. The county, district, and township schools in the area have accumulated arrears of funds, ranging from as much as ten months to as little as seven or eight months. Teachers are struggling to make a living. Before the Dragon Boat Festival, they jointly appealed to the Education Bureau to allocate three months' worth of funds to barely survive. The Education Bureau delayed and did not respond. The day before yesterday, the schools held a joint meeting and, believing that the county government and the County Education Bureau had no sincerity in maintaining the schools, decided to go on strike and issued a declaration. First, it stated that education expenses should not be made difficult when they are not inherently difficult. Second, it criticized the absurdity of levies. Further, it stated the lack of sincerity of the educational authorities. Finally, it asked for the understanding of all elders in the county. On the 19th, a reporter inquired with the Education Bureau, who stated that the Education Bureau had exhausted its efforts and raised 7,800 yuan as a temporary measure. It was tentatively scheduled to issue one and a half months' worth of pay at the end of the month, but the schools could not understand this, so the situation is becoming increasingly serious.

Student Uprising at Suzhou Women's Normal School: Expulsion of the Principal 182

The entire student body of the Suzhou Women's Normal School, because the principal, Chen Shu, dismissed teachers Xu Ruodan, Cao Yangwu, Zhu Bingheng, and Zhai Zhenyuan, sent representatives, including Qian Xiuying, to request Principal Chen to continue hiring them next year. Principal Chen evasively refused, so the students were greatly dissatisfied. In the name of the Student Self-Government Association, they issued a declaration expelling the principal. Principal Chen was once surrounded by students, forcing her to write a guarantee to continue hiring the teachers. The atmosphere was very tense. Principal Chen has submitted this matter to the Education Department for review. Director Peng of the Wu County Education Bureau is very concerned about this disturbance and is already conducting an investigation. If necessary, he may mediate.

(Suzhou, 19th) The entire student body of the Suzhou Women's Normal School is opposing the principal and a storm of expulsions has erupted. Today, they sent eight representatives to the province to petition the Education Department.

Fujian Province Decides to Enforce Literacy as the Central Task of Education 183

(Fuzhou, 18th) Fujian Province has decided to enforce literacy as the central task of education. It has issued a special order to all counties that, when preparing the educational budget for the 24th year and allocating community education funds, it has decided that (1) the allocation of community education funds should account for 15% to 20%. Those who have not met the regulations should find ways to make up the difference and must not misappropriate or reduce funds. If the budget does not comply with the regulations, the Education Department will not put it on record; (2) for any new educational expenses, community education expenses should account for 30% to 50%; (3) increased community education funds should be allocated in the ratio of 30% for urban areas and 70% for rural areas.

Jiangsu Gradually Reduces Funding for Studying Abroad; Remaining Funds are Fully Used for Free Education 184

(Zhenjiang News) The Jiangsu Education Department, having repeatedly received telegrams from the Central Government instructing it to do its best to raise funds from the 24th year onwards to promote compulsory education, should strictly comply. The provincial government committee has already discussed and decided on the funds to be raised by the province for the 24th year. Funds will be allocated separately from the province's special education funds and the province's treasury. Because the province's educational budget for the 24th year has already been established and the use of various expenses has been determined, and new sources of income cannot be raised in a short time, in order to weigh the urgency, it is planned to gradually reduce the funding for studying abroad from the 24th year onwards, and to use all the saved funds for compulsory education. The number that is not enough will be supplemented separately. In recent years, there have been many opportunities for the central government and the Gengkuan (Boxer Indemnity) organization to select students to study abroad. This province is close to the capital and it is easier to participate. After reducing the funding for studying abroad, there will be no major impact. Therefore, a plan to gradually reduce the funding for studying abroad has been drafted and approved by the 751st meeting of the provincial government. The plan is recorded as follows: (1) No more government-funded students will be selected from the 24th year onwards. Those who have been sent will not have their terms extended after they expire. (2) No more subsidized students will be replaced from the 24th year onwards. The current subsidized students will not have their terms extended after they expire. In the 25th year, separate measures will be formulated to reward and subsidize students who study abroad at their own expense, and an amount of 20,000 yuan will be allocated each year. (3) The measures for selecting current education personnel to study abroad will continue to be implemented as usual. According to the above plan, the estimated amount of tuition fees to be paid each year is as follows: (The current calculation book lists 175,000 yuan) In the 24th year, approximately 50,000 yuan should be paid for government-funded students in Europe and the United States, and approximately 25,000 yuan should be paid for subsidies for Europe, the United States, and Japan. Including the funds for researchers and exchange reserve funds, the total cost is approximately 100,000 yuan. In the 25th year, approximately 40,000 yuan should be paid for government-funded students in Europe and the United States, and approximately 3,000 yuan should be paid for subsidies in Europe and the United States. The funds for rewarding students who study abroad at their own expense is 20,000 yuan. Including the funds for researchers and exchange reserve funds, the total cost is approximately 90,000 yuan. In the 26th year, approximately 10,000 yuan should be paid for government-funded students in Europe and the United States. The funds for rewarding students who study abroad at their own expense is approximately 20,000 yuan. Including the funds for researchers and exchange reserve funds, the total cost is approximately 60,000 yuan. From the 27th year onwards, the annual payment for rewarding self-funded students will be 10,000 yuan, the researcher's expenses and other expenses will be approximately 30,000 yuan, for a total of 50,000 yuan.

Ministry of Education Orders Private Medical Colleges in Guangdong to Pay Attention to Improvements 190

The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 18th to the private Guanghua Medical College of Guangdong. The original order stated, "The Ministry has sent personnel to inspect the college. Based on the submitted report and after review, the main points for improvement are presented as follows: (1) The college's funding relies heavily on student tuition and hospital income. The equipment of various special classrooms and practice rooms is rudimentary. In the future, the board of directors should raise funds to strengthen the equipment. In addition, the college's buildings are insufficient for use, and should be built quickly according to the original plan and completed as soon as possible. (2) The equipment in the various departments and operating rooms of the college's affiliated hospital, except for the ophthalmology department, is also mostly imperfect and too focused on business operations, which hinders students' practice. It almost makes the college an affiliated agency of the hospital. Attention should be paid to correcting this malpractice so that the hospital can be fully used for teaching. (3) Most of the teachers in the college's various departments are local practicing doctors and cannot often be stationed at the school. Clinical assistants, each department has as many as three people, while basic science assistants are still lacking. In the future, responsible professors should be added, full-time teaching positions in clinical departments should be established, and basic science assistants should be placed to improve the educational affairs of each department and to earnestly test and train them to improve the students' height. This order is to be followed and improved and reported." The Ministry of Education also ordered the private Xia Ge Medical College the day before yesterday. The original order stated, "The Ministry has sent personnel to inspect the college. Based on the submitted report and after review, the college should make many improvements. The main points are presented as follows: (1) The college's special classrooms and laboratories, and the equipment of the affiliated hospital (except for the obstetrics and pharmacy departments), are generally lacking and should be strengthened immediately to meet the needs of practice and research. (2) The level of students and general subjects is too low. In the future, strict attention should be paid to recruiting new students and training them to improve the level of basic subjects. In addition, foreign teachers lecture in Cantonese, which fails to fully express the theory and needs to be improved. (3) The subjects set up by the college are biased towards the obstetrics and gynecology department. The affiliated hospital restricts the admission of male patients, so students are not given sufficient opportunities for practice. In the future, methods should be found to correct this to facilitate students' practice. (4) There are many staff members in the college. Efforts should be made to reduce them in order to provide the remaining funds for equipment or other beneficial uses. This order is to be followed and improved and reported."

Primary school teaches four subjects: Chinese, mathematics, general knowledge, and English. The time is in the morning. Tuition is not charged for primary school as before, and junior high school only charges four yuan. Board and lodging are available for both male and female students in primary and secondary schools to facilitate students from other places and those who live far away in this city.

Soviet Union - Shooting Breaks World Record 206

(TASS, May 28, Moscow Dispatch) To celebrate the tenth anniversary of "Communist Youth Pravda," the Soviet Union held a national shooting competition on May 24 in Mitishi near Moscow. Participants included 30 shooting athletes from shooting associations in Leningrad, Kiev, Minsk, Ivanovo, Voronezh, Gorky, Kirov, and other places.

The first place was won by Mr. Titov from Ukraine, with 500 points, 494 points. The second place was awarded to Odette Nokov, with 493 points, and Ovchinikov, with 487 points. Mr. Titov broke the world record of Swiss athlete Simmerman, who scored 473 points in the international competition in Antwerp in 1930. On the first day, five people broke Simmerman's world record, and on the second day, another eight people broke this record. Soviet shooters not only broke the world record in the number of hits, but also in their shooting methods. Prushchkiovich's standing shot scored 167 points out of 200 (the previous record was 154), Sishinov's kneeling shot scored 129 points (the previous world record was 168), and Titov's prone shot scored 186 points (the previous world record was 180).

Grains: The Dual Pressure of Flour and Wheat - Silver Tightens, Flour Rots, Mold Rain Arrives - 217

The flour market saw prices for foreign wheat rise, with Chicago up by about 3, 4, or 5 jiao and Canada up by 6 or 7 jiao. Furthermore, both industry insiders and outsiders saw prices holding firm. Opening prices for all months were up by about 1 fen from the previous day. However, after the second round, market sentiment gradually weakened, as retail bulls gradually liquidated positions and new buyers did not emerge. The market atmosphere weakened accordingly. When the market opened in the afternoon, the cloudy weather and cooling temperatures led to expectations of continued rain, and market sentiment turned bearish. Opening prices immediately fell by 1 or 2 fen. Subsequent trading was not active, and both sides largely watched and waited. The market appeared to stagnate. Observing subsequent developments, it may be difficult to see a bullish market due to the tight money supply. As a result, the current month fell by 1 fen and 2.5 li, July and August fell by 2 fen, and September and October fell by 1 fen and 7.5 li.

When the wheat market opened, market sentiment was stable, similar to the previous day. Later, the selling of wheat by domestic groups and the liquidation of positions by bulls led to a gradual weakening of the market atmosphere. When the market opened in the afternoon, the lack of activity in the flour market further softened sentiment. Outside buyers largely watched and waited, as the tight money supply made it difficult to stimulate buying by both industry insiders and outsiders. As a result, prices for July through October fell by 4 fen compared to the previous day. The spot wheat market remained stable, as most of the incoming goods were handled by consignment merchants who were unwilling to sell below cost. Although this year's factory demand was not as greedy as in previous years, market sentiment was still stable. Oil Market: There are Few Hongjiang Tung Oil Hole Goods, Prices Rise 222

Hongjiang Tung oil sales are currently in full swing, but because there are no foreign buyers, price increases and decreases are slow and not drastic. The market is rarely noticed because price fluctuations do not exceed one yuan during the peak sales season in the spring and summer of previous years. Furthermore, the total number of barrels produced by each oil mill in the producing area each year is always over 100,000. Relying entirely on the domestic sales market, the market is often tired for a long time but briefly bullish. However, last year, each oil mill reduced its production in light of excessive inventory. Only 40,000 to 50,000 barrels were produced. By the spring of this year, it was felt that there was not enough to meet sales demand. The shortage of goods became even more serious after the summer, and prices gradually soared. At the beginning of spring, each barrel of vice Hong was only 22 yuan, but by late spring, it had risen to between 25.4 and 25.6 yuan. Recently, as there are fewer goods, the price has become more bullish. The Zhenjiang store opened a public market the day before, with Vice Hong Yang Heng Yuan Qing Yuan Feng two brands requiring 26.2 yuan for Shanghai delivery. Therefore, the store in this port has already sold 26.4 yuan. There is still the Liu Tongqing brand, which used to be reduced by 0.6 yuan, but this year it has increased by 0.2 yuan because the number of productions is the lowest. It needs to be sold for 26.6 yuan. There are also various brands that need to be sold for 25.8 yuan. As for Zheng Hong, such as Jichang and He, the selling price is also the highest because the goods are the best. It is heard that the Zhenxing public market has already sold 31 yuan per barrel, so the Shanghai market will not sell below 31.4 yuan.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

My "National Goods Year" and the Students 224

— Hu Zhaowen

I am a student, and moreover, I am a university student. Of course, I have some connection to the "National Goods Year" for students. However, I insist that I have no connection to the "National Goods Year." What is the reason? Because whether it was before the "National Goods Year" was established or after it was established, whether it was purchasing items or buying clothes, my consistent advocacy and plan to buy and use national goods has never changed. Before this year, I advocated using national goods as much as possible. This year, I still advocate using national goods as much as possible. I had never shouted high-sounding slogans before, and I have not participated in any so-called national goods movements up to this day.

I have never blindly believed in foreign goods, let alone secretly buying or using foreign goods in large quantities. As far as national goods are concerned, I believe that I am ahead of the times, because I have been implementing the work of the so-called "National Goods Year" for students since I was a child. When I entered the first year of university three years ago, I said to my classmates: "I will never wear a Western suit until three days before I go abroad." Although national goods can also be used to make Western suits, they are still rare at the moment.

The work of the "National Goods Year" for students was indeed tense for some time not long ago. The promotion association has also been opened, and earnest speeches and lengthy works of thousands of words are easy to see in newspapers and magazines. However, I dare not believe that the gentlemen who write articles and give speeches are all practitioners who use national goods. Even among the Shanghai students who took a car to the municipal government to take the oath last time, I am afraid that at least a few people wearing foreign Western suits can be found.

Can a movement succeed simply by shouting slogans and giving lectures on reasoning? No! What promotes its success is still the spirit of "hard work". During the "National Goods Year" for students, I hope that students across the country will start from themselves and use national goods and wear national goods. Furthermore, I hope that students across the country will not only use national goods and wear national goods during this year's "National Goods Year" for students, but also regard this year's "National Goods Year" as the meaning of starting to use national goods from this year, and continue to use them forever in the future.

From Inventing National Goods to the Need for Talent 225

— Quan Jia

Recently, there has been a gratifying invention in the national goods industry, that is, Mr. Tianxu Wosheng's self-made pen nib has been successfully announced. After reading the news that the Invincible Pen is about to be launched, we cannot help but admire Mr. Chen, who is striving for national goods. I believe that our national goods industry is hoping for many talents like Mr. Tianxu Wosheng to invent the work of "Heaven Does Not Deceive Me".

Originally, the Chinese seem to be the most fond of imitating. Seeing that a certain industry can be done, you also imitate it, and I also learn from it. As a result, it is crudely made, and the work is reduced, and the things that can be done become impossible to do. In the past, Zhang Xiaoquan's shear shop in Hangzhou was very famous. Not long after, you also called Zhang Xiaoquan, and I also called Zhang Xiaoquan, as if every shear shop had to be called Zhang Xiaoquan to open. It is still the same now. A new Bakelite factory has been established, and after a while, dozens of Bakelite factories have been opened. Of course, everyone thinks that this industry can be done, and everyone is not good at doing this thing. Our national goods industry is often wandering in the diverging road of "imitation" and cannot find the path of creation. This is very worrying!

Let me talk about the importance of inventing national goods again. Many people who love to use national goods are very saddened by the incompleteness of national goods, so they have to use foreign products as substitutes. If there are talents who slowly create the utensils that are not available in the goods and contribute them to the society, I think it will be somewhat beneficial than everyone drilling into an industry and you squeezing me! Moreover, on the one hand, it can prevent the import of foreign goods and make the enemies of national goods be cleared!

However, in fact, there may be many difficulties.

Student Activities During Summer Vacation 226

— Yang An

Summer vacation is approaching. Students of all levels will suspend their studies and return home to spend the summer. I believe that self-respecting students will not let these two months pass in vain. Since this year is the "Student National Products Year," the best approach is to strive to promote the use of domestic goods. How can we do this?

(1) Do our best in our hometowns to promote the benefits of using domestic goods and persuade family members and friends to use domestic goods exclusively.

(2) Investigate the comparison between the sales of domestic and foreign goods in our hometowns. It is best to compile statistics using numerical data to warn the public.

(3) Collect various samples of domestic goods and hold mobile national products exhibitions.

(4) Visit various shops and persuade shop owners to sell domestic goods exclusively.

(5) Hold open-air lectures in the evenings or during the leisure time of villagers to persuade them not to use foreign goods under any circumstances.

(6) Establish a "National Goods Consumption Association" with a fixed charter and solicit local people to join in order to promote the cause.

My respectable and lovable students, this kind of work is most worthwhile and the most valuable way to save the country. Let us all work hard to do it!

Firstly, I am afraid that factories do not have enough capital to fund experimental inventions. Secondly, I am afraid that even if inventions are made, there will be no market for them. Regarding the first point, I hope that the government authorities will cooperate with ambitious domestic goods manufacturers to recruit creative talents on a large scale. Regarding the second point, I implore enlightened customers to abandon their bad habit of buying foreign goods and jointly support the new domestic industry. If my words can serve as a starting point for something greater, that is my hope!

Alas! Eating Foreign Rice! 227

— Zhang Mengzhao

I recently read a news report about our hometown—Wuxi—that truly broke my heart! What was it? It turned out that the rice purchased by the Disaster Relief Committee was entirely foreign rice (Saigon). The checks issued included 5,000 yuan from the Bank of China and 5,000 yuan from the Farmers Bank. Tax-exempt relief rice, already purchased from Shanghai, totaled 6,000 shi (about 600 metric tons) of No. 2 Saigon rice, with each shi costing approximately seven yuan (calculating each shi at seven yuan, 42,000 silver dollars flowed to foreign countries!). Thirdly, more than 30,000 people, large and small, in the 3rd, 5th, 6th, and 7th rural districts were receiving relief due to the drought! Will this relief be sustainable? Will they eat it with peace of mind? I believe this is not a fundamental solution! My old friend, Brother Chusheng, in his commentary in the "Fourth Money Industry Monthly Report" on "Funds Will Be Exhausted by Sitting and Eating," stated, "The outflow of funds continues unabated, and in fact, it is being exported in large quantities. For example, in the case of foreign rice, the imports for two months this year totaled 10,517,783 yuan in national currency. Other goods are not included. These ten million yuan are entirely used to buy rice, and rice is food. Once eaten, it is completely gone! ... If eating it leads to some production, it would not be a waste. Unfortunately, the farmers who have suffered from drought are fleeing to other places, seeking only to be fed and doing nothing... Our country's funds are limited. How can we withstand this waste! As the saying goes, 'Sitting and eating empties the mountain' and 'Eating everything until it's gone!' In the past, this was used to criticize a family or an individual, but now it can be used to criticize the entire society," which is extremely alarming!

My opinion is that we should lend the tens of thousands of yuan in disaster relief funds (silver) to the victims or distribute seeds, and vigorously promote side occupations such as rabbit breeding... (as advocated by my friend Mr. Xue Mingjian, general manager of the Shenxin No. 3 Factory). We should not foster the mentality of sitting and eating relief rice. Even if we purchase, we can use Chinese flour instead. Why must we use foreign rice and send large amounts of silver to foreigners?

Alas! In this booming "Student National Products Year," we are still relying on foreigners for a large amount of what we eat. How can we justify this?

Good News in the Student National Products Year 228

— Ba Ling

Dear students: Isn't this year the "Student National Products Year" as defined by various groups? Although the call to promote domestic goods is still very enthusiastic during the "Student National Products Year," the import of foreign goods is still very fierce and frightening? We can easily understand this if we pay a little attention to the statistics in the newspapers. This situation fills us with endless indignation and heartache!

But, friends, don't be sad. Let me tell you some good news! These are indeed good phenomena and good news in the Student National Products Year, worthy of our joy and congratulations. That is, the industrialist Mr. Tian Xuwo Sheng has invented the domestic steel nib, the domestic economical pen, and Mr. Lin Lubin has invented the domestic eraser, all of which have succeeded one after another. Aren't these some noteworthy good news? Now, I will briefly introduce the three new inventions below, hoping everyone will pay attention.

(1) Domestic Steel Nib

This domestic steel nib was invented by Mr. Tian Xuwo Sheng. Seeing the large sales of foreign steel nibs in Chinese student circles, he resolved to research and invent domestic steel nibs to resist them. After much research and improvement, he has finally succeeded. This pen is G-shaped. In the future, he will also make it in the Polo style. It can also be written on Chinese paper without bleeding. He is actively manufacturing it. Once 100,000 pieces are made, he will announce the launch in the newspaper.

(2) Invincible Economical Pen

This invincible economical pen was also jointly researched and invented by Mr. Tian Xuwo Sheng and Mr. Lin Lubin. The form of the pen is no different from the fountain pens sold on the market, but the nib, pen barrel, and rubber tube are entirely made of domestic raw materials. Its selling price is only about one or two dimes, which is several times less than a fountain pen. It is also being actively manufactured. Once it is made, it will be sold by the Home Industry Society, and students can each have one without paying a huge price to buy foreign fountain pens. Isn't this also a gratifying good news?

(3) Domestic Eraser

Erasers have always been exclusively foreign products. In order to regain rights and interests, Mr. Lin Lubin resolved to create a domestic eraser to meet the needs of all sectors. After much research, he now has a very good product. The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has issued a notice to all schools to purchase it. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce's National Goods Chamber of Commerce has also conducted a thorough review and confirmed that it is entirely a domestic product.

Aren't these three things good news in the Student National Products Year? I sincerely hope that you, dear students, will never buy foreign goods if domestic goods are available from now on. This is how you can be worthy of the hard work of the inventors, and it is also the duty and responsibility of students.

New Inventions in the National Goods Industry 229

— Li Sun

——Mr. Hua’s All-Line China Serge——

Speaking of Nanjing's black satin, people probably know that it was once used as tribute and enjoyed great fame. Therefore, the words "black satin" have left a deep impression on people's minds. During its heyday, the number of workers who depended on it for a living reached more than 200,000; the annual sales were no less than ten million yuan. Its prosperity can be imagined. But unfortunately, since the import of serge and valencia directly from overseas, black satin has suffered a great blow, and now it has fallen into decline. The number of unemployed workers is more than 100,000. This is so unfortunate!

Hua Yutian and his son, who run the Yunchang Weaving Factory at No. 11 Fengyou Temple in Nanjing, are also outstanding talents in the satin industry. Since Nanjing black satin was defeated by imported serge, he has been engaged in the research of weaving serge. After three long years and dozens of failures, he finally succeeded. Now, he has named this serge "All-Line China Serge." It has several advantages: first, the material is smooth and does not attract dust; second, it is durable and does not develop mold spots; third, the material is tough and will not break, and because of its toughness, it is durable; fourth, the price is low. The price of this serge is half the price of imported serge, making it most suitable for making robes, jackets, and shoe materials. Two types have already been woven: one is 2.5 feet wide and 2.5 zhang (about 8.3 meters) long, specifically for making jackets and robes; the other is 5 inches wide, specifically for making shoe materials, with each roll enough to make five pairs of shoes. Hua Yutian and his son have specially contracted with more than a dozen well-known shoe stores in Nanjing, including Lianshengcheng on Sanshan Street, Sanji on Sanshan Street, Sanju on Fudong Street, and Huashengdun on Huapailou, to use China serge as shoe material. He has also applied to the Ministry of Industry for a patent. Hua Yutian and his son also plan to continue researching and weaving All-Line China Serge in various colors. Regarding the research and invention process, according to Hua Yutian and his son, it began in May of the 22nd year of the Republic (1933). First, the serge was disassembled to explore its raw materials and weaving method, and then manufacturing began. However, the woven fabric was not only rougher in texture but also less durable. There were dozens of failures and more than a dozen changes. The changes can be roughly divided into three parts. The first step was to weave silk warp with thread, but the result was that the texture was fine like satin, but not strong. The second step was to use silk as the warp and thread as the weft, but the result was that the texture was too rough. The third step was to weave entirely with silk, which finally resulted in this All-Line China Serge. In total, 70 to 80 bolts of serge were woven since the beginning of the research, and about half of them were not suitable, resulting in a loss of more than a thousand yuan. As for the mental losses, they are simply impossible to calculate.

It is said that the import volume of serge reaches millions of yuan annually. Now that Hua Yutian and his son have invented All-Line China Serge, which is of excellent quality and low price, it can certainly defeat imported serge. This can truly be said to be good news in the Student National Goods Year and is worthy of our solemn introduction!

Attention, Female Students 230

— Ren Fu

The blue cloth that female students wear for their cheongsams (qipao), "Loving-Loving Blue Cloth" (also known as "Modern Blue Cloth"), is generally mistakenly believed to be a domestic product, but its origins are unknown, and the outflow of money is considerable, which is very painful. Now I will briefly describe a thing or two to inform my compatriots. According to the "Loving-Loving Blue Cloth" sold on the market, part of it is Yin Dan Shi Lin cloth produced by a certain foreign company, and most of it is produced by a certain Chinese factory or dyeing factory. There are many brands of blue cloth that falsely claim to be domestic products. Some unscrupulous merchants profit from this by rebranding this kind of blue cloth, or first buying white cloth, dyeing it, and then selling it on the market as entirely domestic products. Its original base cloth is all inferior. If you want to buy genuine domestic products, there are very few. Those who generally buy it fall into the trap. This year is the Student National Goods Year, and I see that female students are all wearing this blue uniform, advising people not to buy foreign goods, but I am afraid that foreigners will laugh their heads off. Here, I recall that the South City Ten Cloth Stores once held a seven-cloth exhibition last year, collecting various kinds of coarse cloth spun and woven by farmers in rural areas, and the products were not bad. A certain female school in South City adopted it as a school uniform, which was quite elegant and admirable, and had the spirit of Gandhi. Many women at home also followed suit. This year, there has been a complete change, and foreign goods have been adopted uniformly, probably because they do not know the inside story and have fallen victim to unscrupulous merchants! (Thank you)

Introduction to Domestic Refined Starch Powder 231

— Meng Zhao

My friend, Mr. Xue Mingjian, general manager of the Shenxin No. 3 Factory in Wuxi, is very enthusiastic about researching domestic industrial arts. Recently, he has also spared no effort in advocating rabbit breeding as a substitute for silkworms! In addition, Yunli Chemical Industrial Company produces a kind of refined starch powder with the "Red Heart" brand. In view of the urgent need to popularize domestic goods, I am happy to introduce it as follows:

Company Introduction: The "Red Heart" brand refined starch powder produced by our company is carefully researched and developed by chemical experts and textile engineers. When used for sizing yarn, it can make the color shiny and increase the tensile strength. When used for sizing cloth, it can avoid the drawback of flooding the cloth surface and can eliminate the need to add butter. Not only can the labor of workers be reduced, but also the cost can be reduced, which is truly good news for domestic factories.

Advantages: Generally, (1) If refined starch powder is not used in the sizing tank, 50 pounds of butter (or up to 80 pounds) must be used. Calculating butter at 18 cents per catty, 4 to 5 yuan can be saved per tank. (2) When refined sizing powder is mixed with butter in the sizing tank, the water must reach a temperature of 70 to 80 degrees before it can be mixed in. If it is put in too early, it may be difficult to mix evenly. If it is put in too late, the sizing power is weak. If this powder is used, it can be mixed in with the sizing and mixed evenly with cold water. Then, the water can be turned on, and it can be used as soon as the water is hot. There is no need to worry about putting it in too early or too late. (3) This powder is completely soluble in water, which can enhance the tensile strength and lubricity of the yarn when dry. It is not only easy to use in the dyeing process, but also saves materials and time!

Spring and Autumn

Snippets 232

— (Lean Scholar)

During the plum rain season, it rains every day and it is also humid, making people feel almost as if they are living in a deep jar. Isn't that suffocating? In the past, people said, "During the plum rain season, it rains in every house, and there are frogs everywhere in the green grass ponds." These two lines of poetry really contain some meaning, because this kind of weather is indeed closely related to farming in our southern regions.

This year, it has been a long time since it rained after summer began. The villagers planted cotton in soil that was like incense ash. How can you expect it to sprout tender leaves? Even if there is a heavy rain soon, it is already too late to replant. People who do not till the land but eat in the cities and metropolises do not know that a famine is coming again.

As the saying goes, "If the summer solstice doesn't come, the water coffin won't open, and cotton will really not grow. Don't even think about planting rice. In our Jiading, it is still 70% cotton and 30% rice," meaning that more people plant cotton and fewer people plant rice. If there is a small harvest, how can we hope for a big harvest? Alas! Human disasters cannot be eliminated. A glimmer of hope originally relied on God's blessings. If the heavens are unwilling to protect us common people, then, I ask, where is the savior!

Hunger 233

— Ni Shanglong

Hunger, the fire of hunger, must be something that everyone fears!

A Confucian scholar of the Song Dynasty said, "Starving to death is a small matter, losing virtue is a big matter." This statement sounds very grand, but it has taken the lives of many people in history. When I was young, I heard my father say that my aunt was a follower of this saying. After my uncle died, she really fasted to avoid losing her virtue, and in just five days, she followed her husband to the underworld!

According to legend, the brothers Bo Yi and Shu Qi fled to Shouyang Mountain to eat ferns because they were ashamed to eat the millet of Zhou. Later, they realized that ferns also belonged to the Zhou family, so they simply stopped eating and starved to death on Shouyang Mountain. I think these two unfortunate brothers were too foolish. Grain and ferns are both born of nature. What does it matter if they belong to the Zhou family or not? Oh! Cursed "Starving to death is a small matter, losing virtue is a big matter!"

Gandhi, the proponent of non-resistance in India, was adept at fasting. This can be seen from the fact that he has fasted many times without starving to death. So, hunger is also an art, with high and low levels. I also thought that Gandhi's fasts were just a form of civil resistance. He hoped to use fasting to move his masters or aristocratic lords. In my opinion, this is slightly more intelligent than the Yi Qi brothers!

Hunger has a long history in China. "Starving corpses line the road" and "Great famine" are indispensable embellishments in the historical books of past dynasties. This cursed hunger is now raging like a wildfire, swallowing countless useful men, women, old, and young.

In the Loquat Orchard 234

— Zhu Shaofei

When the loquats turn yellow, everyone is busy building sheds to watch over them, fearing that they will be stolen or eaten by squirrels and birds. As usual, the pine wood frame that we have erected next to the hall is also removed and moved to the loquat orchard.

The top is covered with reed mats, and the surroundings are covered with reed curtains. Inside, there is a plank, and that patched-up mosquito net is hung, like a small house. The person living inside is safe from the wind and rain.

Day and night, the loquat orchard is lively enough. The sound of oil drums and bamboo clappers resounds in each garden. The birds living in nature are frightened and hide somewhere.

The children are allowed to watch over the shed during the day. At night, I sleep in the shed with my older brother to watch over it, along with that yellow dog.

When we are eating dinner, the yellow dog, who has not been fed, often comes to our feet. His mind knows that food must be taken to the loquat orchard to be eaten. He stares with his eyes, as if urging us to go to the loquat orchard quickly.

My older brother carries the quilt on his shoulder, I light the lantern, and carry the yellow dog's food to the loquat orchard. The yellow dog walks "tat-tat" in front.

The lantern is hung on the eaves of the shed, we arrange the quilt to sleep, the yellow dog eats his fill, licks his lips, and sleeps in front of the shed with his tail tucked in. Gradually, the candle in the lantern burns out, my older brother smokes enough water pipe tobacco before silently falling asleep, and in the quiet garden, one can faintly hear the sound of people knocking on the bamboo clappers in the distance.

Two Sisters 235

— Hua Ling

Although Hu Shansun was not a millionaire, he owned two ancestral stores that were forty or fifty years old, with an annual income of about five or six thousand, so his life was very comfortable.

Although his eldest son was already married and had children, he was still lecherous. Although his wife guarded him like a thief, he would do things like stealing chickens and dogs whenever he had the opportunity.

Three years ago, his hometown was hit by a flood, and poor families sold their sons and daughters in pain. So, Hu Shansun's wife spent 180 yuan, entrusting someone to buy two maids from the countryside. The two maids were sisters. The older one was fifteen years old, and the younger one was two years younger.

In that year, Hu Shansun took a fancy to the older one, and by intimidation and enticement, he got his hands on her, and even got the maid pregnant. Before long, this secret was discovered by Hu Shansun's wife, who gave the maid a thorough beating, almost to the point of death. Needless to say, she also hired a midwife to perform an abortion. As a result, the fetus and the mother both died.

After this incident, Hu Shansun's wife, in order to prevent similar incidents, assigned the younger maid to the eldest daughter-in-law

Records of Fragrant Incense Wafting 236

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

When she had inspected or glanced over the dozens of dishes that had been presented first, she gestured to me, and I, in turn, gave Zhang De a knowing look. Zhang De then softly commanded his trained assistants, "Change them!" Thereupon, these young eunuchs, as orderly, solemn, and swift as soldiers, withdrew the first batch of dishes and brought in the second batch. Immediately, they simultaneously lifted the lids, then turned around and retreated to their original positions, standing stiffly. At this moment, the pungent aroma emanating from the various steaming dishes filled the boat, making everyone's mouth water.

During this time, the orchestras on the other two small boats continued to play softly. I couldn't help but feel a bit touched and began to daydream silently,

"Although I am the daughter of a subject and my status is far below hers, I know what seafaring is like, because I have personally experienced those boundless oceans. I also know how a person sitting in a large ocean liner is tossed about by giant waves beneath them. These magnificent and enjoyable aquatic voyages are infinitely different from messing about in a small boat on Kunming Lake. However, the Empress Dowager, limited by her own position and various court regulations, cannot experience such valuable experiences. Whenever she gets tired of playing on land and wants to be close to the water, she can only float for half a day on this artificial small lake. This kind of small boat pastime, in the eyes of someone like me who has experience crossing oceans, is really too insignificant. It's as if Her Old Majesty and I, as well as others, are a group of naughty children squatting by a small pond playing with water, while our nannies are not far away, carefully watching us, lest we get our clothes wet or fall into the water..." (344)

Odds and Ends

Returning from Visiting the Capital's Air Defense Exhibition 237

— Sun Choucheng

Due to scientific progress and the development of the air force, the mode of warfare has now progressed from two-dimensional to three-dimensional, and the scope of warfare has expanded from the front to the rear. Therefore, aerial defense is now the primary task of national defense. My country's air defense efforts are still in their initial stages, and it will not be easy to succeed without the concerted efforts of the military and civilians. The Air Defense Committee of the National Government's Military Affairs Commission, in view of this, held an air defense exhibition in the capital starting on the sixth of this month in order to arouse public awareness of air defense and to popularize air defense knowledge. Choucheng happened to be in Beijing on that day due to a petition from the new medicine industry, and visited the exhibition the next day. Therefore, I have recorded what I saw below:

The opening ceremony venue was the public stadium, which can accommodate more than 20,000 people. At night, outdoor movies on air defense issues were shown in the stadium. The exhibition hall was set up in the First Park, and connected to the stadium. Above the towering archway at the entrance was a silver model airplane, with the couplet: "A country without air defense facilities cannot survive in today's world." "A populace with a self-defense organization is sufficient to cope with modern warfare." Behind the Sun Yat-sen's will monument, a bomb model was specially erected, measuring four meters long and weighing two tons, which made people shudder. Next to it was a billboard more than a foot square, depicting the tragic scene of a city being bombed by airplanes, which was shocking to the eye. It instantly reminded me of the disaster in Zhabei during the January 28th Incident, and I almost shed tears. Inside the First Exhibition Hall of Wandering Leisurely, there were various "photos of surveying and testing equipment" and "diagrams of the evolution of warfare." On a three-foot-long table, dozens of airplane models were placed, with detailed lists of their names, styles, performance, size, weight, etc., clearly marked in front of each plane, making them easy to understand at a glance. The anti-aircraft barrage balloon net had different styles. The one displayed in the hall was a net-shaped suspension type. Inside the reed shed were "artillery camouflage nets" and "parachutes." The former was covered with yellow mud and green grass, so that enemy planes would not know that artillery was hidden there when scouting from the air. The latter was twenty-four feet in diameter, divided into twenty-four folds, and connected to the belt by twenty-four silk ropes, which were used when jumping from the air. It was made of domestic silk fabric, which was even more commendable. There was also a board, divided into eight grids, which statistically showed the number of military aircraft in various countries around the world. A five-inch-long airplane model was nailed to each grid, with one plane representing one hundred. France had the most, with fifty planes nailed on, while Poland had the least, with ten planes nailed on. Other countries, such as the United States, Russia, Britain, Italy, Japan, and Germany, were arranged in order. From a distance, they looked like hundreds of dragonflies resting there. To demonstrate the effectiveness of anti-aircraft guns, a two-foot-high wooden platform was made, with anti-aircraft guns of various styles arranged around it, all pointing upwards. An airplane was electrified, causing it to fly in the air, and the mouths of the four guns moved back and forth with the plane, which was very ingenious. Various bombs were dissected and accompanied by explanations, in different sizes. The second exhibition hall was in the Geopolitics Society, displaying an ideal model of urban air defense facilities. The surveillance, intelligence, and alarm room, the blocking zone, the firing zone, the listening zone, and the surveillance zone were all determined by the distance from the center. In the basement, the houses were winding and fully equipped, serving as a bomb shelter during wartime. The third exhibition hall was in the Martyrs' Shrine, with a modern female model wearing a gas mask. Her mouth was three inches long, similar to Zhu Bajie in Journey to the West, which attracted the attention of the audience. Next to the rescue room was a human body model of a person who was killed by a bomb because he did not apply for air defense. His right ear and left leg were injured by the bomb, and the flesh was blurred, which was horrible to look at and lifelike. The park area was vast and had marked routes, so even though there were crowds of people, they were still orderly.
